
-----title
合肥 (出生地)
-----detail

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=1036')">999-1036年</a>，1-38岁</div><div id='17d9512138144988bfb9e464bf04f047' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=1000')">999-1000年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　居乡，其妻董氏出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1011')">1002-1011年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年</a>　居乡，其父包令仪任福建惠安县知县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1022')">1013-1022年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　居乡，少刻苦读书。时文彦博之父泊与包拯之父令仪同官阁中，拯与文彦博方业进士，交友深厚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1026')">1024-1026年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年1月</a>　进士及第。初授大理评事、知建昌县，续改监和州税，因父母春秋高，遂解官侍养。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1031')">1028-1031年</a>　居乡，奉养父母。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　母张氏卒，拯庐墓守丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　除服，家居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1036')">1034-1036年</a>　居乡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3de48233f35d4126bee052dbe27bb543_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3de48233f35d4126bee052dbe27bb543");'><span id='3de48233f35d4126bee052dbe27bb543_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1054')">1053-1054年</a>，55-56岁</div><div id='3de48233f35d4126bee052dbe27bb543' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　丧子，乞便郡，得知扬州，旋改庐州。亲旧有扰官府者，绳之以法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　知庐州。请求免除高阳路欠负。作品：请放高阳一路欠负。<div id='poem_1158483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请放高阳一路欠负奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐五年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158483")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158483'>臣昨任高阳关日，以部下十一州军诸般欠负，并系明堂赦前，合该除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158483_comment'></div>缘逐州军从前失于举行，臣寻具欠折因依，保明申奏，乞与除放，已蒙三司送本路转运司，再令勘会，至今未尽结绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158483_comment'></div>况前件欠负，委是逃亡人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158483_comment'></div>其閒或有存者，又无家业抵当，即不是侵欺盗用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158483_comment'></div>今又该南郊大赦，欲望朝廷特赐指挥，检会臣前状，尽与除放。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　知庐州。迁刑部郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　任刑部郎中、知庐州。韩琦曾上《乞罢诸路里正》作品：请罢里正只差衙前。<div id='poem_1158492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢里正只差衙前奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158492")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158492'>臣伏见知并州韩琦上言，乞罢诸路里正，逐乡税赋只委户长催纳，三司已牒逐处转运司相度去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158492_comment'></div>臣昨任河北，备见诸州军所差里正，只是准备衙前，其秋夏二税，并是户长催驱，重役之中，里正为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158492_comment'></div>每县或无上等，即以中等户充，家业少有及百贯者，须充衙前应副重难之役，例皆破荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158492_comment'></div>其逃亡非命者，比比皆是，怨嗟愁苦，所不忍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158492_comment'></div>今若依韩琦起请悉罢里正，如衙前有阙，即委令佐于一县诸乡第一等中选差物力最高者充役，如更有阙，亦如此轮差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158492_comment'></div>委是经久公私利便，庶几凋残之民稍获存济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158492_comment'></div>又缘里正系正月内差，若伺候诸路转运司相度，必恐迟延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158492_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特赐详酌，早降指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158492_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f542f0cf74da41f5a32312763ed3010f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f542f0cf74da41f5a32312763ed3010f");'><span id='f542f0cf74da41f5a32312763ed3010f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>，65岁</div><div id='f542f0cf74da41f5a32312763ed3010f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年8月</a>　女婿文效护丧归，葬于合肥县公城乡公城里。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
天长
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4188266af289432a8cefeeb850786c6c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4188266af289432a8cefeeb850786c6c");'><span id='4188266af289432a8cefeeb850786c6c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1039')">1037-1039年</a>，39-41岁</div><div id='4188266af289432a8cefeeb850786c6c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　毕亲丧，重新出仕，知扬州天长县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　知扬州天长县。察割牛舌盗，官迁大理寺丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1039')">1038-1039年</a>　知扬州天长县。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
肇庆（高要）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9844586bd6244ed9824c7f638b0d5be8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9844586bd6244ed9824c7f638b0d5be8");'><span id='9844586bd6244ed9824c7f638b0d5be8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1042')">1040-1042年</a>，42-44岁</div><div id='9844586bd6244ed9824c7f638b0d5be8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　徙知端州，官迁殿中丞。病民之汲于江，凿七井以便其用。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　知端州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年3月9日</a>　知端州。与提点刑狱周湛、同提点刑狱钱聿游端州城北石室大岩（即七星岩），并题名留念。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年冬</a>　知端州任满，由朱显之接任。任满不持一砚归，律己之义凛乎严凝。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='34119f2ff1f647e88f05a37c097187ff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("34119f2ff1f647e88f05a37c097187ff");'><span id='34119f2ff1f647e88f05a37c097187ff_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1045')">1043-1045年</a>，45-47岁</div><div id='34119f2ff1f647e88f05a37c097187ff' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年春夏间</a>　入朝任勾当京东排岸司官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年11月</a>　因权御史中丞王拱辰推荐，拜监察御史里行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　任监察御史里行。因睹其时“官吏升陟，贤否相混，世族补荫，愚智不分”，认为治乱之源，在于慎取贤士。作品：论取士。<div id='poem_1158381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论取士奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158381")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158381'>臣以孤远之迹，猥荷圣选，擢升宪府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158381_comment'></div>退思所以为报，则智识蒙浅，无以副上旨之万一，敢竭愚见，唯明主裁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158381_comment'></div>臣伏睹近降诏敕，以官吏升陟，贤否相溷，世族补荫，愚智不分，并立新条，以革旧弊，有以见陛下求治垂训之深旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158381_comment'></div>臣闻天下，大器也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158381_comment'></div>群生，重畜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158381_comment'></div>古之圣王，御大器，保重畜，盖各有其道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158381_comment'></div>以万务之无极也，一统于上，岂可以思虑尽之邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158381_comment'></div>故立三公，设九卿、百执事，以维持之，俾群材尽力，而百工无旷，则王者正其本，执其要，而天下之大务举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158381_comment'></div>故治乱之原，在求贤取士得其人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158381_comment'></div>《汉书》云：「帝王之德莫大于知人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158381_comment'></div>大抵斯人之情，皆希荣进，莫不饰正于外，藏邪于内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158381_comment'></div>邪正所蕴，渊密难辨，而审之必有术焉：以贤知贤，以能知能，知而用之之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158381_comment'></div>且知人与不知人而任之，乃得失所系，而安危从之，宜乎取士之际不可不慎焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158381_comment'></div>夫三代取士之法，阔略难议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158381_comment'></div>两汉而下，莫若唐天宝之制，自京师逮郡县，皆有学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158381_comment'></div>每岁仲冬，馆学课试，乃与计偕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158381_comment'></div>其不在馆学而举者，谓之乡贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158381_comment'></div>并责成有司，唯以得之与否为荣辱，得士者升，失士者黜，孰不公其心以进退乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158381_comment'></div>其得第者，但谓之选人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158381_comment'></div>有格限未至，而能试文三道者，谓之宏词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158381_comment'></div>试判三道者，谓之拔萃，中是选者，得不限年而授职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158381_comment'></div>复有贤良之科焉，所以区别才行，慎重名器，如是之审也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158381_comment'></div>故当时文物尤盛，比隆三代，基构绵远，垂三百年，其有繇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158381_comment'></div>今之取士则异于是：乡曲不议其行，礼部不专其任，但糊名誊本，烦以绳检，复于轩陛，躬临程试，三题竞作，百篇来上，不逾三数日，升降天下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158381_comment'></div>其考较去留，可谓之精且详乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158381_comment'></div>臣亦恐非进贤退不肖之长策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158381_comment'></div>《周礼》升秀辨官，司徒、司马、大乐正之职，未闻王者躬其事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158381_comment'></div>议者谓：不若近约唐制，归诸有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158381_comment'></div>或曰：取舍之柄，当繇人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158381_comment'></div>曰：盍使礼部考试，定其可否高下，混于奏籍，赐第上前，抑亦无失于国体矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158381_comment'></div>然后复宏词、拔萃之科，明立条目，宽限人数，岁一设之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158381_comment'></div>其与选者，比类奏举之人，以次甄擢而任之，有以得其实才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158381_comment'></div>顷年虽复贤良、拔萃之科，得人裁一二而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158381_comment'></div>又罢拔萃之举，恐未足尽魁梧之选也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158381_comment'></div>且今之仕者，非保任则无以自进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158381_comment'></div>若参以二科而精求之，则取人之路岂不裕乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158381_comment'></div>而又佥举之敝渐不可长，其閒或昵于爱私，或迫于势要，不得已因而举之者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158381_comment'></div>缪滥无别，宜一警革，若至其甚，何所及焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158381_comment'></div>方今天下多事，边鄙未宁，政失于宽而弊于姑息，士弛于务而幸于因循，固宜推择真贤，讲求治道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158381_comment'></div>外则黜郡守县令不才贪懦苛虐之辈，以利于民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158381_comment'></div>内则辨公卿大夫无状谄佞朋比之徒，以肃于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1158381_comment'></div>杜绝回邪，振张纪律，可使教惇于上，民悦于下，足以导迎和气，驯致太宁，不亦盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1158381_comment'></div>伏望陛下稽前代之成败，验当今之得失，政有未顺，理有未安，则思而图之，图而行之，行而终之，则生灵受其福，而宗社享无疆之休矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1158381_comment'></div>惟陛下鉴其区区，恕其狂直，一赐观采。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1158381_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　任监察御史里行。此年十一月初二日夜，上清宫火。拯上疏请求勿再修缮。作品：请不修上清宫。<div id='poem_1158493' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158493' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158493?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请不修上清宫奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158493")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158493_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158493'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158493'>臣伏见十一月初二日夜上清宫火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158493_comment'></div>谨按《春秋传例》曰「人火曰火，天火曰灾」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158493_comment'></div>《汉书·五行志》曰「人火、天火，同为灾异」，皆以朝廷政令参验得失而劝戒焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158493_comment'></div>说者曰：贤佞分别，官人有序，则火得其性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158493_comment'></div>若信道不笃，或耀虚伪，则火失其性，自上而降，滥燄妄起，是为火不炎上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158493_comment'></div>今上清宫者，乃祖宗修建以崇无为之德，今火燔之者，岂焚修之人不务精洁，以副陛下严奉之旨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158493_comment'></div>不然，其天意垂诫于陛下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158493_comment'></div>固宜励精治道，谨修人事，以答天变可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158493_comment'></div>风闻道路云：陛下存留道众，似有缮修之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158493_comment'></div>未辨虚实，咸怀危惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158493_comment'></div>况天下多事，调发旁午，帑藏未实，边鄙未宁，岂可先不急之务，重无名之率哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158493_comment'></div>且宫观之兴，自于唐室，非古制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158493_comment'></div>若谓先圣真容理当钦奉，则景灵宫、会灵观殿宇宏壮，可以奉安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158493_comment'></div>愿陛下推仁慈之德，念疲敝之俗，且务安之之理，岂忍重困之也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158493_comment'></div>然外议纷纭，颇甚惑众，欲乞特降诏告谕，以安众心。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1158493'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158493'><span class='label'>按：</span>包拯于皇祐二年至四年知谏院。《续资治通鉴长编》卷一五四庆历三年十一月丙寅「上清宫火」注：「监察御史包拯有章乞勿修。」据改。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1158493_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年冬</a>　任监察御史里行。针对时权贵子弟调任州郡长官情况，提出不任县令者不得为按察官、通判、知州。作品：论县令轻授。<div id='poem_1158417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论县令轻授奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年为监察御史里行时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158417")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158417'>臣闻古之所重，为民父母者，县令耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158417_comment'></div>今之所贱，而不能振起风教者，亦县令耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158417_comment'></div>盖擢用之际，未精其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158417_comment'></div>凡有清流素望，或稍挟权势之人，即苟谋他官，耻为县道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158417_comment'></div>但庸人下品，甘于其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158417_comment'></div>虽郡隶吏卒，皆能诃制，茍免罪戾之不暇，欲振起风教，为民父母，其可得乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158417_comment'></div>且今朝廷仕进清选，大臣子弟偶缘文墨，或希辟命，即自下僚擢升馆职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158417_comment'></div>不然，才出外任，列为佥判，不繇为县，便作通判、知州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158417_comment'></div>洎为长吏，昧于民情，懵然其閒，不知治道之出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158417_comment'></div>况四方多务，令长尤在得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158417_comment'></div>欲乞今后贴职并佥判及京朝官，凡历仕中不曾任县令及知县者，不得便为长吏按察之官，且令知县方得入通判、知州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158417_comment'></div>如此，则宰邑得其人，长吏亦不能倖求而至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　任监察御史里行。时范仲淹等条陈十事，其四“择官长”。针对推举出的官员不能及时上任之问题，拯提出要随举随用，不拖延，不冗繁。作品：请先用举到官。<div id='poem_1158382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请先用举到官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158382")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158382'>臣伏睹近者降敕节文，委中书、枢密院选举主二十人，令举堪充知州、通判、知县各一员者，盖国家精择良吏之深旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158382_comment'></div>所有内外被举之人，至今未见擢任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158382_comment'></div>兼访闻逐路转运使，累有体量到州县长吏等，其閒不才贪猥之尤甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158382_comment'></div>欲乞所举人内，先次进用，令往彼冲替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158382_comment'></div>若候人数足日，方议差除，则疲乏之民受害深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158382_comment'></div>况幅员至广，官吏至众，黩货暴政，十有六七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158382_comment'></div>若有急于用人，以革其弊，亦朝廷之深忧，不可不察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1158382_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158382'><span class='label'>按：</span>《包拯集》卷二。又见《历代名臣奏议》卷一三三，《古今图书集成》铨衡典卷一九、选举典卷五二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1158382_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　任监察御史里行。时右侍禁李用和应募杀“军贼”张海，而朝廷未按事前所立赏格封赏。作品：论李用和捉获张海乞依赏格酬奖。<div id='poem_1158379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158379?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论李用和捉获张海乞依赏格酬奖奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年冬）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158379")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158379'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158379'>臣闻功疑惟重，乃国之令规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158379_comment'></div>赏不踰时，欲人之知劝：抑先圣之格训，又驭邦之大柄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158379_comment'></div>伏见朝廷先以军贼张海等未获，特立赏格，召募使臣，如捉获，依傅永吉例，优加酬奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158379_comment'></div>近闻右侍禁李用和应募而往，不踰数旬，果能杀获张海等四人，馀众并已溃散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158379_comment'></div>用和授东头供奉官、閤门祗候，中外闻之，无不失望，似非朝廷开示大信之旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158379_comment'></div>且张海一岁之内，恣行残暴，京西十馀郡，幅员数千里，官吏逃窜，士民涂炭，以至江淮州县，无不震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158379_comment'></div>前后凡遣使臣，悉多败衄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158379_comment'></div>臣窃谓张海之害，甚于王伦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158379_comment'></div>用和之功，优于永吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158379_comment'></div>而永吉左班殿直、閤门祗候，凡超八资，授诸司副使、宣事舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158379_comment'></div>今用和止超四资，功同赏异，何以激劝将来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158379_comment'></div>且有明文，岂宜降等？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158379_comment'></div>况西鄙未定，盗贼閒起，方当责效之际，不可失信于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158379_comment'></div>其李用和欲乞依准元降指挥，比类傅永吉，特与优改官秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158379_comment'></div>如此，上之出令贵乎必行，下之立功乐于自奋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158379_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年8月</a>　由监察御史里行迁为监察御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年3月</a>　任监察御史。范仲淹等人推行“庆历新政”，其《详定贡举条制》中有“不封弥誊录”条文。作品：请依旧封弥誊录考校举人。<div id='poem_1158383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请依旧封弥誊录考校举人奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158383")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158383'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158383'>臣伏睹新定贡举条制节文，诸州发解，令知州、通判、职官、令录等保明行实，更不封弥誊录者，此乃三代里选之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158383_comment'></div>盖朝廷欲先德行而后词学，责成有司，不欲烦以绳检，庶取士有以得其实才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158383_comment'></div>缘天下郡学自罢听读之后，生徒各以散去，一旦诏下，投牒求试者比比皆是，长吏等又安能一一练悉行实哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158383_comment'></div>不免祇凭逐人递相保委，然而诈伪猥杂者亦无由辨明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158383_comment'></div>兼每州用试官一员，是天下试官逾三百馀员，必恐未能尽得其人，而悉心于公取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158383_comment'></div>或缘其雅素，或牵于爱憎，或迫于势要，或通于贿赂，势不得已因而升黜者有矣，又何暇论材艺，较履行哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158383_comment'></div>洎取舍一谬，则是非纷作，不惟抑绝寒素，窃虑天下因此构起讼端多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158383_comment'></div>况封弥誊录，行之且久，虽非取士之制，稍协尽公之道，若今来诸州发解举人，且令仍旧封弥誊录考校，于理甚便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158383_comment'></div>若以敕命方行，难于遽改，即乞特降约束，其逐处试官、监试官如稍涉徇私及请托不公，并于常法外重行处置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158383_comment'></div>不然，合别定刑名，庶使官吏等各知警惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158383_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年夏</a>　任监察御史。江淮等地自去秋至今春，三时亢旱。作品：请免江淮两浙折变四章。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文凡四章，前两章分别作于庆历四年4月9日、4月28日，后两章稍后奏上。）</span><div id='poem_1158471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请免江淮两浙折变奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　权三司使时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158471")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158471'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158471'>臣窃见淮南、江浙、荆湖等州军，数年以来，例皆薄熟，去秋亢旱尤甚，可熟三二分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158471_comment'></div>当年夏税见钱，一例科折：内第一等折纳小绫，每疋一贯六百六十文省，官绢每疋二贯八百五十文省；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158471_comment'></div>其第二等已下至客户，并折纳小麦每斗三十四文省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158471_comment'></div>续据发运司准中书剳子，据三司奏，乞将庆历三年上供额斛斗六百万石内，将小麦一百万石、大豆十五万石折纳见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158471_comment'></div>发运司遂相度小麦，每斗并耗添估九十四文省，大豆每斗并耗八十八文省，比逐处见粜价例两倍已上，应该小麦一石纳见钱九百四十文省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158471_comment'></div>寻又准五月九日中书劄子，据发运司奏，窃虑豆麦价高，人户难得见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158471_comment'></div>奉圣旨宜令本司疾速指挥，逐路州军据合折夏税豆麦，令人户如愿纳见钱者，即仰逐处依起纳日在市价例钱数送纳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158471_comment'></div>如只愿纳本色斛斗，亦听从便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158471_comment'></div>虽有前件圣旨指挥，本处官吏并不遵禀，但一面抑令人户纳元估价钱，不许纳本色斛斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158471_comment'></div>以致豆麦益贱，钱货难得，下等人户尤更不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158471_comment'></div>发运司但务岁计充盈，不虑民力困竭，上下相蒙，无所诉告，为国敛怨，莫甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158471_comment'></div>且民者，国之本，财用所出，安危所系，而横赋暴取，不知纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158471_comment'></div>若因此流亡相应而起，涂炭郡邑，则将何道可以卒安之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158471_comment'></div>况已萌之兆，不可不深虑耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158471_comment'></div>兼自淮以南及两浙、荆湖从去秋至今春，并未得雨，二麦不秀，耕种失时，民心嗷嗷，日怀忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158471_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降诏敕，委逐路转运、提刑不住巡历体量，应是诸杂科率，权且停罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158471_comment'></div>若向去蚕麦稍熟，今年夏税诸色钱等，除第一、第二等户各令依旧折纳外，其第三等已下并客户，特与免诸般支移折变，只令各纳本色，庶使重困之前稍获苏息。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1158471_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请免江淮两浙折变奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158472")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158472'>臣近曾上言，以江淮、两浙、荆湖等州军，自去秋至今春，未得大段雨泽，二麦不秀，耕种失时，并去年诸处夏税，一例折纳见钱，小麦每斗估价九十四文省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158472_comment'></div>民閒钱既窘迫，麦又无用，应急贱粜纳官，其直每斗不过三二十文，中等已下人户，绝更不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158472_comment'></div>今又时雨稍愆，蝻蝗复作，民心愁苦，深可矜悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158472_comment'></div>况东南奥壤，国家仰之如帑府，尤宜保固，以制诸夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158472_comment'></div>若不急于优恤，继之以重困，兽穷则攫，窃恐更为朝廷之忧尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158472_comment'></div>臣先乞应系诸般科率，权且停罢，如将来蚕麦丰登，中等以下且令各纳正税、本色钱等，权免今年折变，庶孤贫人户稍获苏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158472_comment'></div>至今多日，未蒙指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158472_comment'></div>欲乞检会，速赐施行，兼乞下诸路转运司、提刑司，不住巡历体量，或有蚕麦不熟之处人户申䜣，州县不得抑退，并令依例疾速差官检覆，开破逐色租税，免致流亡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158472_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请免江淮两浙折变奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158473")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158473'>臣昨于四月九日剳子上言，以江淮、两浙、荆湖等州军自去秋至今春，未得大段雨泽，其中等以下人户，夏税乞不依去年折变见钱，令只纳本色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158473_comment'></div>又于当月二十八日上殿剳子，亦乞令中等以下人户权免今年夏税折变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158473_comment'></div>至今多日，未蒙指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158473_comment'></div>兼诸处见今纳夏税，若令一例折变，深属不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158473_comment'></div>缘逐路今岁蚕麦薄熟，雨泽久愆，耕种失时，蝻蝗复起，秋成未保，人心益怖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158473_comment'></div>而又民閒钱货绝难出办，若不特赐宽恤，窃虑下等不济人户，以官钱窘迫，必致流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158473_comment'></div>强壮者尽为盗贼，老弱者转死沟壑，不独搔扰郡邑，抑亦离去畎亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158473_comment'></div>矧国家财用所出，尽在东南，不得不深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158473_comment'></div>又访闻京东、京西、河北、河东、陕西今夏蚕麦例皆丰熟，此乃天意欲少宽东南之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158473_comment'></div>若此数路稍旱，调度或急，则朝廷纵有矜悯之心，亦无所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158473_comment'></div>然臣职贱言轻，宜无采录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158473_comment'></div>但事体至大，乞留圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158473_comment'></div>伏望陛下特出宸断，速赐指挥，则一方生灵有再苏之望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158473_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请免江淮两浙折变奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158474")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158474'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158474'>臣近者累次上言，乞江淮、两浙、荆湖等州军，中等已下人户，今年夏税权免诸般折变，祇令各纳本色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158474_comment'></div>寻奉圣旨，送三司相度，访闻三司已具申奏讫，至今未降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158474_comment'></div>缘诸路见纳夏税多日，兼有路分绝远之处，若更稽缓，窃虑后时，即陛下矜恤之心恐无所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158474_comment'></div>伏望圣慈悯此重困之民，速赐指挥，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1158474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年夏</a>　任监察御史。时陈州去冬遇大雨雪，故庄稼收获欠佳。作品：请免陈州添折见钱。<div id='poem_1158475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请免陈州添折见钱奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158475")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158475'>臣访闻知陈州任师中昨奏，为本州管下五县，自去冬遇大雨雪，冻折桑枣等，并今年春蚕只及三五分，二麦不熟，全有损失去处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158475_comment'></div>除擘画不放省税外，只乞与免支移折变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158475_comment'></div>已奉圣旨，令京西转运司相度闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158475_comment'></div>窃知本路转运司牒陈州，令将今年夏税大小麦与免支移，只令就本州送纳见钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158475_comment'></div>却令将大小麦每斗折见钱一百文，脚钱二十文，诸般头子仓耗又纳二十文，是每斗麦纳钱一百四十文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158475_comment'></div>况见今市上小麦每斗实价五十文，乃是于灾伤年分二倍诛剥贫民也，则民閒钱货从何出办？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158475_comment'></div>兼将客户等蚕盐一斤，一例折作见钱一百文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158475_comment'></div>又将此一百文纽做小麦二斗五升，每斗亦令纳见钱一百四十文，计每斤土盐却纳三百五十文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158475_comment'></div>况一郡五县数十万口，非常暴敛，小民重困，体实非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158475_comment'></div>欲乞特降指挥，令本州疾速依见今在市二麦实价，估定钱数，令民取便送纳见钱，或纳本色，庶使东辅近地不济人户，稍获苏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158475_comment'></div>兼虑本路应系灾伤州军，或有似此重行折变之处，亦乞特行勘会，速赐指挥，若少稽延，恐无所及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158475_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。庆历和议后，西夏向北宋称臣，元昊复遣杨守素来议事。拯反对议和。作品：论杨素守。<div id='poem_1158514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论杨守素奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158514")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158514'>臣伏见西贼再遣杨守素诣阙请命，而朝旨方议纳其诚款，此亦安民御边之长策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158514_comment'></div>风闻道路云：元昊欲岁纳青盐，贸易茶货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158514_comment'></div>然未审虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158514_comment'></div>缘元昊数州之地，财用所出，并仰给于青盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158514_comment'></div>自用兵以来，沿边严行禁约者，乃困贼之一计尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158514_comment'></div>今若许以岁进数万石，必恐禁法渐弛，奸谋益炽，不惟侵夺解盐课利，亦虑浸成大敝，关防或未能制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158514_comment'></div>若稍行捉捕，则弃前恩，结后怨，此亦必然之势也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158514_comment'></div>议者复欲令运于关东支用，或许客人稗贩，则又不免配率车乘，转成搔扰，固朝廷所宜慎重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158514_comment'></div>此举如不获已，则不若于前来许赐帛缯茶货数量与增加，亦可以弭亡厌之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158514_comment'></div>兼此剧贼猖狂难保，沿边塞栅备御之具，亦不可少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158514_comment'></div>缘臣疏外之职，素不预议，但采于物论，知所以然，敢罄公言，少裨万一。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年6月</a>　任监察御史。时魏兼于部内置业，并剩量过职田斛斗，已下法寺详断”，拯上疏要求重断，以警贪猥。作品：请法外断魏兼。<div id='poem_1158429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请法外断魏兼奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年夏）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158429")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158429'>臣访闻勘到前淮南转运使、工部郎中魏兼，以先在任日，于部内置买物业，并剩量过职田斛斗等罪犯奏案，已下法寺详断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158429_comment'></div>魏兼早践周行，荐叨烦使，专总察之任，在表率之地，故当正身莅下，竭节奉公，而乃不顾朝章，自为非法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158429_comment'></div>窃虑疏决在近，乞不从原减之例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158429_comment'></div>臣伏见先朝以崔端知华州日，于部下创置物产，事发被劾，先帝置之散秩，摈弃终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158429_comment'></div>其魏兼，伏望圣慈特出宸断，法外重行，以警贪猥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年盛夏</a>　任监察御史。因出榜召到蔡州驻泊都监阎士良罪状87状，拯请疾速理勘，一就结案。作品：请勘阎士良。<div id='poem_1158459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请勘阎士良奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年盛夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158459")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158459'>臣伏见许州通判、太常博士张士安奏，准敕赴蔡州制勘驻泊都监阎士良与知州陈述古互相奏论，兼准敕连陈述古状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158459_comment'></div>据官员人吏僧尼等首，阎士良强买骡马牛羊，及乞取钱物，共七十五状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158459_comment'></div>并据士良论述古私役兵士，恣横不公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158459_comment'></div>其出榜召到陈首阎士良八十七状，不敢一例根勘，已送本州及申奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158459_comment'></div>窃缘阎士良、陈述古互论不法事件至多，所出榜召到陈首阎士良八十七状，亦合画时行遣，不合却送本州，显属避事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158459_comment'></div>欲乞特降指挥，令本勘官将所召到陈首士良八十七状，疾速理勘，一就结案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158459_comment'></div>兼访闻一行干连人数不少，炎酷方炽，缧系颇久，罪非本犯，情实可悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158459_comment'></div>且干连人等，应系照證，各有归著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158459_comment'></div>如该杖罪已下之人，亦乞令本处一面先次决遣疏放，盛暑之际，免淹刑禁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年7月</a>　任监察御史。拯提出整顿吏治，对刻薄好进、苛酷官员“屏而不用”作品：请不用苛虐之人充监司二章。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此疏第一章上于庆历四年七月，至八月乙卯前奏上第二章。欧阳修曾上疏《论台官所言按察使不当》驳斥包拯之言。）</span><div id='poem_1158411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请不用苛虐之人充监司奏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158411")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158411_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1158411_0'>① 一　庆历四年七月为监察御史里行时作</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158411'>臣窃见诸道转运司自兼按察及置判官以来，并提点刑狱等，体量部下官吏，章疏相继，颇伤烦碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158411_comment'></div>兼闻审刑院、大理寺日近奏案尤多，倍于往年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158411_comment'></div>况无大段罪名，并是掎摭微累，不辨虚实，一例论奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158411_comment'></div>孤弱无援者则按以深文，权势豪猾者则纵而不顾，内则徇一身之利以殖其私，外则窃振职之名以图其进，效尤无耻，惟恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158411_comment'></div>至有公清守节之人，或不曲事左右，为众所嫉者，即被加诬，构成其罪，遂使守己之士或负终身之玷，可不痛惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158411_comment'></div>且治平之世，明盛之君，必务德泽，罕用刑法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158411_comment'></div>故董仲舒曰：「阳为德为春夏，当和煦发生之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158411_comment'></div>阴为刑为秋冬，在虚空不用之处」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158411_comment'></div>以此见天任德不任刑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158411_comment'></div>王者亦当上体天道，下为民极，故不宜过用重典，以伤德化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158411_comment'></div>昔暴世法网凝密，动罹酷害，下不堪命，卒致溃乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158411_comment'></div>《老子》曰：「其政察察，其民缺缺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158411_comment'></div>其政闷闷，其民淳淳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158411_comment'></div>臣愿圣明鉴于此言而无忽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158411_comment'></div>方今民力凋残，国用窘迫，若乃专用刻薄好进之吏，则民不聊生，窃恐非国家之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158411_comment'></div>虽朝廷累降诏命约束，罕或遵禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158411_comment'></div>此弊不去，为患寖深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158411_comment'></div>欲望圣慈宣谕执政大臣，应转运、提刑等并令精选廉干中正之人，以充其职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158411_comment'></div>苛细矫激之辈，屏而不用，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158411_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158411'><span class='label'>按：</span>《包拯集》卷四。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷六七，《历代名臣奏议》卷一三三，《古今图书集成》铨衡典卷一九、祥刑典卷一○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1158411_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1158412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请不用苛虐之人充监司奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　庆历四年八月作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158412")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158412'>臣先曾上言，以诸道转运使自兼按察及置判官以来，并提点刑狱等，体量部下官吏，颇伤烦碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158412_comment'></div>兼审刑院、大理寺奏案尤多，倍于往年，况无大段罪名，并是掎摭微累，不辨虚实，一例论奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158412_comment'></div>此盖茍图振举之名，以希进用之速尔，遂使天下官吏各怀危惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158412_comment'></div>其廉慎自守者，则以为不才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158412_comment'></div>酷暴非法者，则以为干事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158412_comment'></div>人人相效，惟恐不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158412_comment'></div>民罹其患，无所诉告，殆非陛下委任之本意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158412_comment'></div>其被体量之事，或智虑所不及，或人情偶不免，若非切害，亦可矜悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158412_comment'></div>虽欲改过，其路亡繇，岂不痛惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158412_comment'></div>兼访闻天下茶盐酒税，逐处长吏曲徇转运使之意，以求课额羡溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158412_comment'></div>民则例遭配买，商旅则倍行诛剥，为国敛怨，无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158412_comment'></div>且朝廷设按察、提刑之职，盖欲去贪残之吏，抚疲瘵之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158412_comment'></div>今乃务为苛细，人不聊生，窃恐未为国家之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158412_comment'></div>比者幸属郊禋盛礼，大霈庆泽，欲乞于敕书特行约束，凡官吏先被体量者，情非重犯，咸许自新，后或不悛，必置于法，庶使悔过之人免负终身之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158412_comment'></div>其诸处茶盐酒税，亦乞除元额外不得擅增课利，搔挠人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158412_comment'></div>应系自来诸般调率，且乞权罢，以安海内生灵之心，伏望圣慈少赐省察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158412'><span class='label'>按：</span>《包拯集》卷四。又见《续资治通鉴长编》卷一五一，《古今图书集成》铨衡典卷一九、祥刑典卷一○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1158412_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年8月</a>　任监察御史。拯要求朝廷从重处罚张可久贩私盐，以儆效尤。作品：请重断张可久。<div id='poem_1158426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请重断张可久奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年八月为监察御史时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158426")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158426_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158426'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158426'>臣等伏见佥书武信军节度判官厅公事吴奎奏勘，前淮南转运按察使、司勋郎中张可久招伏，不合在任日于部下兴贩私盐一万馀斤等情，罪案下大理寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158426_comment'></div>窃虑本寺引用应犯违禁等物，并以见捉获斤两条贯定断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158426_comment'></div>今张可久贩私盐已经卖过，别无见在，议罪必轻，况前件条贯，本为细民所设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158426_comment'></div>按张可久本庸鄙之资，滥按察之任，为朝廷之倚重，乃一方之表帅，而巧图财利，冒犯禁宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158426_comment'></div>虽前后职司臣僚或有以赃滥获罪，然未有如可久之甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158426_comment'></div>此而可恕，孰不可容！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158426_comment'></div>其张可久乞不原近降疏决，特于法外重行远地编管，以励将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158426_comment'></div>仍乞今后应臣僚等或犯兴贩诸般违禁等物者，不以见在或废用，并以元犯斤石罪名定断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158426_comment'></div>其诸色人等所犯，即依旧条施行，所贵贪猥之辈，稍知警惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158426_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年8月</a>　任监察御史。庆历四年八月初五日，保州兵乱。作品：论保州事。<div id='poem_1158515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论保州事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158515")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158515'>臣伏见保州城内兵士等自杀害官吏以来，朝廷累行招谕，及一面进兵攻取，至今固守未下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158515_comment'></div>况地据要害，境接虏界，兼访闻虏中见屯兵界上，以防托为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158515_comment'></div>其安肃军、广信军切须以宿将重兵镇守控扼，以备侵轶之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158515_comment'></div>且兵家之法，惟务神速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158515_comment'></div>今若用兵进讨，则城坚难拔，降敕招谕，又人心未信，倘不别议措置，必恐变故难测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158515_comment'></div>此诚事机危迫之秋也，固不可以寻常容易处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158515_comment'></div>欲望圣慈于内臣选择素有材辩可任者，令赍密诏往彼，缒入城中，以诏旨一二亲自宣谕，俾逆党知朝廷并贷前罪，普与昭洗之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158515_comment'></div>纵逆党迷惑，未即信从，其閒诖误胁从之人，以使命在彼，必有他变，或翻然改图矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158515_comment'></div>昔唐德宗朝，李怀光据河中叛，累命将帅攻城不下，乃以给事中孔巢父及中使持诏入城慰抚，未久，部将牛俊斩怀光以城降，此亦前事之可验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158515_comment'></div>若但以诏敕于城外招安，缘此辈自知恶逆罪不容诛，亦未审朝廷确然推诚信宽贷之恩，以城壁坚固，粮食充足，且务偷生茍延月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158515_comment'></div>虽欲必取，又缘诸处卒伍素不训习，攻城之具亦旋创造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158515_comment'></div>不惟进攻之后，城中生聚枉遭涂炭，兼恐兵士等所伤必甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158515_comment'></div>万一别有他虞，事体不小，尤不可不深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158515_comment'></div>以臣博采外议，若令亲信内臣赍诏入城，谕以赦宥，许其自新，事必可济，于理亦便<span class='inlineComment2'>（《包拯集》卷九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158515_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1158515'>庆历四年八月：原无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158515_comment'></div>此奏言保州兵变事，考《续资治通鉴长编》卷一五一、一五二，庆历四年八月保州云翼军据城叛，至九月辛酉<span class='inlineComment2'>（三日）</span>平，是此奏乃八月上，据补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。庆历四年七月契丹遣使者告伐夏国，八月宋遣余靖报使契丹。作品：论契丹事宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　任监察御史。八月余靖使契丹回，拯反对赐契丹誓书，主张稍缓与之议和。未成。作品：论昊贼事宜。<div id='poem_1158513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论昊贼事宜奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158513")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158513'>臣窃闻余靖近进北虏回书，其意未顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158513_comment'></div>今杨守素朝辞将发，未审朝廷如何处置？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158513_comment'></div>今若纳元昊诚款，仍赐誓书，窃恐北虏因之得以为词，于理未便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158513_comment'></div>缘北虏结好四十年矣，事无纤钜，莫不徇从，一旦骤违其意，非计之得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158513_comment'></div>况事体至大，若不出于成算，岂可容易拟议哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158513_comment'></div>设欲恃北虏之旧好，纳西戎之新款，纵无后患，亦防他变，得此失彼，恐未为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158513_comment'></div>万一虏情忿戾，乘衅而动，则曲在我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158513_comment'></div>驩盟一失，迫悔何及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158513_comment'></div>此乃系国家安危之机，可不慎乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158513_comment'></div>兼知元昊先所陈请，或未尽从，且可再令商量，稍缓其事，数月之内，彼中事机尽见，然后图之，惟陛下特赐省察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158513_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　任监察御史。时保州兵马监押韦贵降充岳州监税，拯言其罪大责轻，当重行处置。作品：乞断韦贵二章。<div id='poem_1158421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞断韦贵奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　庆历四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158421")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158421'>臣伏睹宣命，以权保州兵马监押供奉官韦贵降充岳州监税，中外闻之，无不惊愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158421_comment'></div>况韦贵当兵士构叛之时，不能死节，为其戎首，同恶相济，致朝廷用兵攻取，累降诏谕，方且开门纳款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158421_comment'></div>今若酬其后效，特贷深刑，此而可容，孰不可恕！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158421_comment'></div>夫人臣无将，将则罪死无赦，且将有其意，尚无可免之理，况悖逆之状如是之甚乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158421_comment'></div>兼闻韦贵尝发妄言，激成逆志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158421_comment'></div>迨凶徒之窃发，叶奸计以图全，悖理乱常，天下共弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158421_comment'></div>及王师之进讨，据坚城而请命，要求抚纳，以盖前愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158421_comment'></div>质诸神祇，所难容舍，致之刑辟，允为得宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158421_comment'></div>设欲从轻免其孥戮，只乞于远恶处安置，亦朝廷屈法推恩之宽典也<span class='inlineComment2'>（《包拯集》卷四。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158421_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1158421'>庆历四年九月：原无，据《续资治通鉴长编》卷一五二所载此事补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158421_comment'></div>下篇同。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158421_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞断韦贵奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　庆历四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158422")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158422'>臣近者上言，以新降充岳州监税韦贵，欲乞重行处置，以伸国法，至今未奉指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158422_comment'></div>窃缘保州云翼兵士，见谋背叛，戕贼长吏，固守城壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158422_comment'></div>其巡检使王守一、走马承受刘宗言不从逼胁，相继遇害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158422_comment'></div>而韦贵不能死节，仍助凶威，主领叛徒，凡二十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158422_comment'></div>劫夺财物，戮辱良善，一城生聚，死者几半，以至登陴拒守，屡抗王师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158422_comment'></div>及攻具外合，众心内溃，窜伏无路，方乃开门请命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158422_comment'></div>要君怙乱，无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158422_comment'></div>朝议录其罪愆，使图后效，免死为幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158422_comment'></div>况冒难致死者，曾未甄录，而同恶相济者，又不诛责，臣窃恐无由奖激忠义而垂诫将来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158422_comment'></div>其韦贵如未欲便行严断，即乞于远处编管。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158422_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。蒋堂推举前保州通判石待制不当，罚铜四十斤。拯言责轻不足以诫滥举者。作品：请重坐举边吏者。<div id='poem_1158423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请重坐举边吏者奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年秋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158423")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158423'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158423'>臣伏睹近降敕命，以枢密直学士知益州蒋堂为奏举前保州通判、秘书丞石待举不当，罚铜四十斤，放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158423_comment'></div>按石待举残虐屯兵，刻削廪食，群凶相扇，固守城壁，杀害民吏，几成大患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158423_comment'></div>原其情状，免死犹未塞责，而保任之者，止从轻典，窃恐不足以诫其滥举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158423_comment'></div>缘河朔三路，军民财赋，事务繁剧，长吏僚佐，尤在得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158423_comment'></div>所以申命近臣，同罪保举，盖国家慎重选擢，如是之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158423_comment'></div>而论荐之人，不能体认朝廷求实才，备急用之意，但缘其雅素，或昵于爱私，或追于势要，或通于贿赂，势不得已，因而举之，又何暇论材器，较治行之详悉哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158423_comment'></div>致一旦用之，为国生事，不可不深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158423_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后应河北、陕西、河东知州军、通判、兵马都监已下，依旧令两制以上臣僚，举曾历三路差遣，谙悉边事京朝官及武职等，委是精当，方得以次选用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158423_comment'></div>如擢用后稍不如举状，并乞同坐，重行朝典。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158423_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时晏殊罢相，拯建言慎择贤才任相。作品：晏殊罢相后上。<div id='poem_1158369' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158369' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158369?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晏殊罢相后上奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158369")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158369_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158369'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158369'>臣闻帝王之德，莫大于知人，知人则百僚任职，天工无旷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158369_comment'></div>夫宰相者，上佐人主，以道治天下，固非庸材所堪，当历选群卿，以补其阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158369_comment'></div>得其人则舆议厌伏，非其人则大职堕斁，治乱之本，在兹一举，可不慎之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158369_comment'></div>臣伏见晏殊罢免，朝廷必再命相，此乃陛下慎择贤材之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158369_comment'></div>况今百度或阙，生民未泰，契丹、夏贼，交臂伺边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158369_comment'></div>宰相得人，则可以上尊朝廷，外威夷狄，陛下庶宽宵旰，垂拱仰成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158369_comment'></div>若但取左右毁誉，容易以付大柄，恐非国家之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158369_comment'></div>况近臣才与不才，皆圣心所尽知，在裁之圣断，勿牵群疑尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158369_comment'></div>臣非次不敢求上殿进对，惟陛下特留圣意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158369_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年冬</a>　任监察御史。时孙甫言丁度有罪，丁上疏求皇帝辨明。然仁宗对丁度奏折未予答复，拯乞各与辨明。作品：论丁度孙甫事乞辨明。<div id='poem_1158446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论丁度孙甫事乞辨明奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年冬）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158446")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158446'>臣等窃闻翰林学士承旨丁度累上劄子，称于召对日奉圣旨面谕，右正言孙甫言度会上殿求入两地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158446_comment'></div>今丁度乞赐辨證，至今未见指挥，物议喧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158446_comment'></div>窃缘任用大臣，出于圣断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158446_comment'></div>如丁度实曾上殿妄自求进，颇失事体，或孙甫所言虚诳，中伤近列，即乞各与辨明，特赐行遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158446_comment'></div>且丁度、孙甫俱处侍从之班，日被顾问，今互有论列，未辨曲直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158446_comment'></div>若朝廷姑务含容，不行降黜，则好进者无所警惧，言事者得以离閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158446_comment'></div>疑惑圣听，隳紊朝纲，无甚于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158446_comment'></div>欲望圣慈将丁度累上文字，早赐降出施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年冬</a>　任监察御史。庆历四年十一月，蛮贼于连、韶州界处打劫。作品：论蛮贼事二章。<div id='poem_1158519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蛮贼事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158519")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158519'>臣窃见广南东路钤辖司奏：据连州申，勘到行者孙之道称，蛮贼等三千馀人商量入连州打劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158519_comment'></div>勘会彼中兵甲数少，已差奉职周僧辩带兵甲一百人前去防托者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158519_comment'></div>缘广南英、韶、连、贺四州，并与湖南郴、衡、道、永等州相接，自蛮贼骚动以来，彼处稍有备拟，虏略无得，贼计必谓岭南无备，有侵轶之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158519_comment'></div>兼闻八月九日，蛮贼五百馀人打劫连州桂阳县两村人户财物牛马不少，今来贼势转盛，所差兵级数少，必难枝梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158519_comment'></div>况广南州郡并无城壁及攻守之具，加之兵力绵薄，无堪用者，若不速议措置，使此贼得便乘虚深入，曷以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158519_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降指挥，下本路转运、钤辖司，令于逐州界首可控扼之处，相度添置寨栅，屯兵防托，以警备之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158519_comment'></div>不然，恐为患转大，贻朝廷之深忧也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1158519_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蛮贼事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158520")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158520'>臣窃闻广南东路钤辖司奏，蛮贼三千馀人入连州界打劫，杀害人命及使臣等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158520_comment'></div>并转运司奏，乞差禁军及选有将略武艺使臣前来防托捉杀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158520_comment'></div>臣先曾上言，以连、贺、英、韶等州最与荆湖南路接界，窃虑蛮贼以岭南无备，乘虚深入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158520_comment'></div>缘彼中州县，并无城壁及攻守之具，兵力绵薄，山路险阻，缓急救援不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158520_comment'></div>乞于逐处要害可控扼之所，相度创置寨栅，屯兵守把。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158520_comment'></div>今蛮贼累次打劫，其势稍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158520_comment'></div>若不令速剪灭，为患不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158520_comment'></div>如候朝廷差拨禁军，恐无所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158520_comment'></div>缘北人乍到，不谙风土，多染瘴疫之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158520_comment'></div>窃见唐时或岭南叛扰，并自江西起兵进讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158520_comment'></div>况虔、吉等州疆境相接，民俗颇同，若选差使臣往彼抽发兵士，或召募就近应副，事体至便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158520_comment'></div>地里不远，人必可用，欲望速降指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时张若谷年近八十，仍不致仕。作品：弹张若谷。<div id='poem_1158451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158451?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹张若谷奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158451")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158451'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158451'>臣闻引年致政，抑有定规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158451_comment'></div>殉禄贪荣，颇伤清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158451_comment'></div>窃见龙图阁直学士、兵部侍郎、知洪州张若谷，年近八十，自登膴仕，亟践清涂，久越既耄之年，未有乞骸之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158451_comment'></div>虽圣朝眷待近侍，进退以礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158451_comment'></div>而大臣去就之义，安可罔然不知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158451_comment'></div>伏况江西重地，为一都会，兵赋繁盛，控扼上游，尤在得人，以之镇靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158451_comment'></div>兼检会御史台先有起请，乞行颁示；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158451_comment'></div>而张若谷未能引退，尚此冒居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158451_comment'></div>人之寡廉，一至于是！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158451_comment'></div>欲乞申明前命，谕之致仕，或与别移一郡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158451_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时兴国寺僧鹿皮道者绍宗多行恶端，拯建言严惩此辈。作品：请安置鹿皮道者。<div id='poem_1158439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请安置鹿皮道者奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158439")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158439'>臣闻善为国者，必务去民之蠹，则俗阜而财丰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158439_comment'></div>若蠹原不除，治道从何而兴哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158439_comment'></div>窃见兴国寺僧鹿皮道者绍宗，自残支体，稔怀奸诈，扇诱聋俗，聚集凶党，创修寺宇，镕铸佛像，糜费货宝，不知纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158439_comment'></div>方国家多事，财用窘急，岂容此辈恣行掊刻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158439_comment'></div>且佛者觉也，在乎方寸，假有万像之广，不出五蕴之中，但平等慈悲，即成正道，有为功果，非所崇尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158439_comment'></div>昔唐朝欲造大像，狄仁杰上疏论列，即时罢役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158439_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下俯矜庶品，博采群议，凡所兴造，速赐禁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158439_comment'></div>其僧绍宗，亦乞于外处安置，庶免惑众。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时仁宗以“内降”之法宽赦罪犯周景，破坏法纪。作品：论内降周景札子。<div id='poem_1158425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论内降周景劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158425")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158425'>臣访闻军巡院见勘周景，为于庆历二年五月，系内东门手分，发意同胡可观与杂买务同情盗用罗帛等入己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158425_comment'></div>事发，其杂买务监专并该决配，内周景为首，合得绞，胡可观为从，流配千里外牢城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158425_comment'></div>其周景避罪逃走，三司寻具申奏，乞不原赦减降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158425_comment'></div>至三年三月内捉获，奉圣旨决脊杖十七，配黄州牢城，为患未决；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158425_comment'></div>本州不详前来指挥，却原赦减降决臀杖十七，为患未区分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158425_comment'></div>昨驾船上京，遂告嘱造军器及北作坊手分等，指射充本坊皮匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158425_comment'></div>近押赴省司，断先寄杖数，遇夜未决，依前逃走，寻已捉获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158425_comment'></div>窃闻奉传宣劄子，令免徒罪，只配北作坊工匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158425_comment'></div>缘周景原情至重，减死已优，若更免刑，深属长恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158425_comment'></div>况可观为从，尚该徒配，岂可为首之人却全免罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158425_comment'></div>刑罚一滥，则狡吏得以为奸，无所畏惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158425_comment'></div>欲乞圣慈特降指挥，下三司子细根勘，依元降徒罪，更不令充工匠，改配远地州军牢城收管，所贵顽猾之辈不能幸免。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158425_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时冬雷震发，雨木成冰，有巨嵎之震。拯建言要谨慎对待，不可忽视。作品：谨天戒。<div id='poem_1158365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谨天戒奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158365")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158365'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158365'>臣窃见近者太白犯月于箕尾之分，荧惑犯镇星于虚、危之分，而又冬雷震发，雨木成冰，博询前闻，固不虚发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158365_comment'></div>臣谨按历代《五行志》曰：太白犯月，月犯太白，荧惑犯镇星，皆外寇之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158365_comment'></div>雨木成冰者，说者谓上阳施不下通，下阴施不上达，故雨木为之冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158365_comment'></div>冰者阴之盛，木者少阳贵神，卿大夫之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158365_comment'></div>亦曰：木冰为木介，介者甲兵之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158365_comment'></div>又曰：冬雷者，所发之地主兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158365_comment'></div>谓雷以二月出，八月入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158365_comment'></div>今季冬而震雷雨雹者，阳不闭藏而发泄，皆失节之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158365_comment'></div>夫月者太阴之长，后妃大臣诸侯之象，亦主夷狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158365_comment'></div>镇星所管宋、卫、陈、郑之分，若金火凌犯，固不为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158365_comment'></div>况又箕尾属燕，虚、危属齐，设或内非其应，则北虏之患，山东之忧，亦须大为之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158365_comment'></div>且顷岁有星孛之异，近复有巨嵎之震，不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158365_comment'></div>今四方灾旱，流亡未复，虽遣使绥抚，贷粟赈给，而上下困竭，济恤攸艰，此乃天意笃佑圣宋，丁宁陛下如是之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158365_comment'></div>《书》曰：「历象日月星辰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158365_comment'></div>此言王者当仰视天文，俯察地理，观日月消息，候星辰躔次，揆山川变动，参人民谣俗，以考休咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158365_comment'></div>若见灾异，则退而责躬，恐惧修德以应之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158365_comment'></div>有不可救者，则蓄储备以待之，故宗社享无疆之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158365_comment'></div>伏望陛下省灾异之来，验休祥之应，谨奉上天之戒，以揆当世之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158365_comment'></div>外则幅员之广，戎狄寇盗之可虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158365_comment'></div>内则机政之繁，号令赏罚之未信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158365_comment'></div>固宜进擢贤杰，振张纪律，广辟众正之路，屏绝群枉之门，斥远奸憸，慎重听纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158365_comment'></div>近自宫禁，远及边陲，杜渐防微，中外协济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158365_comment'></div>如此，则庶几后患可弭，惟圣度裁处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1158365_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。针对招募宣毅军时存在问题，提出“互换屯驻”之法。作品：论宣毅军。<div id='poem_1158502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论宣毅军奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158502")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158502'>臣窃见近年天下添置宣毅指挥，以为郡县之备，诚不可阙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158502_comment'></div>然初议招募之时，例物稍厚，故民閒无状积恶之辈，悉投名籍中，官吏等又急于数足以邀旌赏，岂暇一一选择？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158502_comment'></div>今来所在屯聚，乃大为州郡之害，骄悍狂悖，结成群党，与效尤相扇，动不能制，凡有小可差使，亦不敢用，例皆姑息之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158502_comment'></div>今海内无事，此辈尚敢如此，若缓急驱之御寇，焉肯用命，不为祸首幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158502_comment'></div>况前后作过伤害官员不少，若不早为处置，必恐浸成大患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158502_comment'></div>其逐处宣毅兵士，欲望特行指挥，令分擘于诸州互换屯驻，所贵散其凶党，免贻后悔，仍乞特降宣命，严赐约束，应有罪犯，并行决配。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1158502_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。庆历初宋夏战事不息，朝廷曾下诏臣僚举贤人，合并充河北、陕西、河东三路知县。拯乞各与改差本路知县。作品：论先举三路知县不得令监当。<div id='poem_1158416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论先举三路知县不得令监当奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158416")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158416'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158416'>臣伏睹先降敕节文，以河北、陕西、河东知县，比之诸路，民赋边备，岁计不少，尤须得人，委臣僚选择廉勤干事之人，于前任职官令录内同罪保举充京官知县者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158416_comment'></div>自降敕文之后，臣僚或有保举之人，并降告敕，于本任改京朝官，仍于本处待阙，候逐路有知县员阙，即便就差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158416_comment'></div>盖朝廷以边鄙未宁，财用不足，安民集事，尤在得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158416_comment'></div>所以委群僚精择良吏，不循常格，就转优秩，用绥疲俗，以济调度之深旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158416_comment'></div>其所举之人，祇合并充三路知县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158416_comment'></div>访闻数内著作佐郎魏及甫，见监河中府白家盐场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158416_comment'></div>大理寺丞唐叔夏，见监并州军资库；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158416_comment'></div>大理寺丞何澄，见督并州永利监；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158416_comment'></div>著作佐郎叶仲馆，见监沧州盐山税；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158416_comment'></div>著作佐郎董之邵，见知坊州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158416_comment'></div>臣细详敕意，为比逐路税赋科率稍重，诸县阙人，是以不次甄擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158416_comment'></div>其前项官显是不合差于逐处监当并知录，深属不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158416_comment'></div>其魏及甫等，欲乞依应元敕，各与改差本路知县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158416_comment'></div>切恐更有似此不系亲民者，亦乞勘会，一例移改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158416_comment'></div>所冀繁剧之邑，庶可责成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158416_comment'></div>侥倖之人，免或避事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1158416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时普遍存在提点刑狱失职渎职问题，拯提出针对大辟死罪或有过审判期而未决之案，提刑官应亲自审问决断。作品：请令提刑亲按罪人。<div id='poem_1158420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请令提刑亲按罪人奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（为监察御史里行时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158420")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158420'>臣伏见国家设按刑之司，盖虑郡县长吏或不得人，刑罚冤滥，俾之纠察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158420_comment'></div>而大狱出入，未尝按问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158420_comment'></div>细故增减，即务举劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158420_comment'></div>是小过必察，而大罪不诃，何以副圣人钦恤之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158420_comment'></div>今敢略举一二以明之：臣昨任端州日，狱中重囚七人，具案已就，适会提刑司巡历将至，闻其未断，即迁延引避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158420_comment'></div>又邻近春州禁勘罪人，追捕甚众，缧系二百馀日，凡该大辟罪者四五人，徒罪不少，亦不闻提刑司推究淹延之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158420_comment'></div>洎转运司取公案委官定夺，果有失入死罪等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158420_comment'></div>虽官吏悉行重典，而死者不可复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158420_comment'></div>窃恐天下刑狱，似此冤枉者至多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158420_comment'></div>虽前后累降诏敕丁宁，罕或遵守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158420_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后诸州凡勘大辟罪不以军贼百姓五人已上并出违日限者，并委提刑司画时亲往审问决断，所冀刑狱无或冤滥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158420_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。建言广南知州，不可轻授，应选有知县经验、政绩好、有官员保举者。作品：请选广南知州。<div id='poem_1158390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选广南知州奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158390")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158390'>臣窃见广南应系知州，例差奏荫京朝官初任知县及一考者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158390_comment'></div>伏况世禄之胄，鲜惇义教，童孺之岁，便忝仕籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158390_comment'></div>未尝学政，即使司民，甫越期年，又移典郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158390_comment'></div>且一邑之事尚未练悉，六条之重安可责成？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158390_comment'></div>地虽远僻，不可轻授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158390_comment'></div>方国家多务，调率旁午，远民困重，尤在得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158390_comment'></div>臣前任端州日，具知其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158390_comment'></div>或无职官处，只是知州独员管勾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158390_comment'></div>其猥冗恣横之辈，则惟务诛求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158390_comment'></div>庸懦懵昧者，又全不晓事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158390_comment'></div>民罹其害、无所诉告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158390_comment'></div>提刑、转运使惮其远恶，复不能巡历按劾，但上下相蒙耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158390_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后奏荫京朝官合该广南知州者，并于次任知县内选有治绩及举主者，方得差移，并乞勘会元无职官处，各选置一员，仍令转运、提刑司非时不得差出，所贵关掌郡事，辑宁异俗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时广南知州、县令缺员。作品：请广南添差职官二章。<div id='poem_1158404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请广南添差职官奏<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158404")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158404'>臣昨上言，以广南诸州乞今后应奏荫京朝官，合该往彼知州，并于次任知县内，选有治迹及举主者，方得差移，并乞勘会东西两路，元无职官处，各选置一员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158404_comment'></div>至今多日，未蒙朝廷施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158404_comment'></div>窃缘岭服之表，地最遐僻，俗性犷悍，易动难安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158404_comment'></div>今又蛮贼猖狂，郡县搔挠，长吏之任，尤在得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158404_comment'></div>况童孺之年，未尝学政，不当轻授，重困远民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158404_comment'></div>且近地牧守，尚有通判职官，更相裨赞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158404_comment'></div>而岭外远郡，乃令此辈独员管勾，民罹其害，无所控告，甚非朝廷求治之本意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158404_comment'></div>兼访闻所阙职官，祇二十馀州，每州各置一员，事理至便，所贵关掌郡务，以安异俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158404_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，令检会臣先进劄子，速赐施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158404_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158403?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158403'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158403'>臣先曾上言广南东西两路诸州，原无职官处，各令置一员，关掌郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158403_comment'></div>寻蒙降指挥下铨司，至今未闻有人注拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158403_comment'></div>虽该赦恩放选，又例注家便及次远，以岭外遐僻，惮其地远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158403_comment'></div>兼访闻两路阙员甚多，其十数年无正官处，并差土人充摄官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158403_comment'></div>缘近年蛮贼侵挠，民力困竭，全藉廉干官吏多方绥抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158403_comment'></div>今来铨司若候合入远选人及情愿者，窃恐卒未差除得人，深属不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158403_comment'></div>窃见顷岁以来，广南阙官，遂于江浙就移两任四考以上簿尉，充彼处县令，自后因循不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158403_comment'></div>欲乞特降指挥，令铨司检详旧例，于江浙、荆湖等处近便路分诸州簿尉中，选无公私罪犯，两任五考已上就除权职官，四考已上就除县令，便令赴任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158403_comment'></div>如此，则远官无由倖免，异俗得以辑宁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。时封驳制度名存实亡，拯提出恢复封驳的具体建议。作品：请复封驳。<div id='poem_1158380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请复封駮奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158380")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158380'>臣伏见朝廷近日凡有除授，制命已行，或物论未允者，则臣僚上疏论駮，因而追改者有之，然未若精择而后用之之审也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158380_comment'></div>故外议喧然，谓进退可否之柄不专于上，流闻四方，大损国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158380_comment'></div>且两汉而下，并以左曹给事中领駮正之任，李唐尤重其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158380_comment'></div>若擢用未当，则论列于内，不显扬于外，盖不欲明君之过，沽己之直也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158380_comment'></div>近代则不然，但建一策，议一官，则必扬言于朝，以为己功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158380_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158380_comment'></div>为臣之道，岂当如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158380_comment'></div>窃睹国家循旧例置门下封駮司，以近臣兼领，未尝见封一敕，駮一事，但有封駮之名，而无封駮之实，因循不振，岂不惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158380_comment'></div>且历代典故沦废多矣，此局幸而未坠，祇在举而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158380_comment'></div>臣请特正封駮之职，选两制以上慎重介直不挠者主之，或命谏官兼掌，应有除授之制，并先由门下，其不可者，得以辨别是非，封进诏敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158380_comment'></div>如此，则差易改正，兼免漏泄，少裨圣政。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。为劝赏廉吏，警示贪官，请求不任用赃吏。作品：乞不用赃吏。<div id='poem_1158405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不用赃吏奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（为天章阁待制知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158405")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158405'>臣闻廉者，民之表也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158405_comment'></div>贪者，民之贼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158405_comment'></div>今天下郡县至广，官吏至众，而赃污擿发，无日无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158405_comment'></div>洎具案来上，或横贷以全其生，或推恩以除其衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158405_comment'></div>虽有重律，仅同空文，贪猥之徒，殊无畏惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158405_comment'></div>昔两汉以赃私致罪者，皆禁锢子孙，矧自犯之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158405_comment'></div>太宗朝尝有臣僚数人犯罪，并配少府监隶役，及该赦宥，谓近臣曰：「此辈既犯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1158405", 1158405, "Clauses/22/Comments/1")'>赃滥</span>，只可放令逐便，不可复以官爵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158405_comment'></div>其责贪残、慎名器如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158405_comment'></div>皆先朝令典，固可遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158405_comment'></div>欲乞今后应臣僚犯赃抵罪，不从轻贷，并依条施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158405_comment'></div>纵遇大赦，更不录用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158405_comment'></div>或所犯若轻者，只得授副使上佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158405_comment'></div>如此，则廉吏知所劝，贪夫知所惧矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　任监察御史。京东等地暴发小规模农民起义、士兵暴动。拯提议及时安抚平定。作品：请差京东安抚二章。<div id='poem_1158431' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158431' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请差京东安抚奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158431")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158431_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158431'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158431'>臣闻京东、河北两界州军，见今贼盗充斥，并畿内东明、襄邑等县，亦有劫贼，并未捕获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158431_comment'></div>虽已选差武臣，窃恐结集转多，为患不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158431_comment'></div>兼访闻东路州军，以近年科率差役频并，民力困重，不逞之辈，因而啸聚，所在窃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158431_comment'></div>况曹、兖、沂、淮阳等州军，山林深远，素号出剧贼之所，不可不令即时诛灭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158431_comment'></div>顷岁京东、西军贼等作过，差侍御史仲简、监察御史蔡禀监督捕捉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158431_comment'></div>今欲乞选差台官一员，乘传往逐处体量民閒疾苦，假以便宜，俾之抚绥，兼督责州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158431_comment'></div>所贵官吏效命，不敢顾避，速得剿除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158431_comment'></div>其逐处长吏兵官等稍畏懦者，亦乞精择有方略强干臣僚对替，庶免败事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158431_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158469' class='_poem'><div
