id='poem_title_1158469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再请差京东安抚奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158469")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158469'>臣近以京东盗贼充斥，曹、兖等州长吏，乞别选差有方略臣僚，及遣台官一员，往彼体量安抚，监督诸州县捕捉，免成后患，未蒙指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158469_comment'></div>缘京东素是出强贼处，不可不即时诛灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158469_comment'></div>若令结成群党，藏伏山林，则为害不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158469_comment'></div>况巨嵎山累年震动，去春兖、郓又地震，兼春前岁星孛于虚危之次，亦是齐分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158469_comment'></div>此皆变异之大者，固不虚发，不可忽天戒而不大为之防也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158469_comment'></div>且前代并本朝，天下凡有灾伤盗贼，即遣黜陟使或采访、安抚等使循行郡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158469_comment'></div>今之议者必谓虚有烦费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158469_comment'></div>若其得人，可以按察官吏能否，询访民閒疾苦，俾之便宜从事，所济岂不大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158469_comment'></div>所有本路转运使，亦未甚振职，乞于别路对换有才略者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158469_comment'></div>不然，则败事，虽悔无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158469_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特许检会臣先进剳子所乞近差曹、兖等州长吏，并差台官安抚事，早赐施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年3月</a>　任监察御史。考试奏荫子弟，是“庆历新政”措施之一，于庆历三年十一月颁行。时欲废止。作品：请依旧考试奏荫子弟。<div id='poem_1158384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158384?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请依旧考试奏荫子弟奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历五年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158384")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158384'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158384'>臣伏睹先降敕节文，应奏荫子弟京官年及二十五以上，其选人遇南郊大礼，限半年内许令赴铨投状，京官每年春季国子监投状，并差两制官于逐处考试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158384_comment'></div>内习词业者，或论或诗赋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158384_comment'></div>习经业者，各专一经，试墨义等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158384_comment'></div>及格者与放选、注官及差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158384_comment'></div>自敕下之后，天下士大夫之子弟莫不靡然向风，笃于学问，诏书所谓非唯为国造士，是乃为臣立家，实诲人育材之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158384_comment'></div>近闻有臣僚上言，欲议罢去，是未之熟思尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158384_comment'></div>且国家推恩之典，其弊尤甚，因循日久，训择未精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158384_comment'></div>今诏命方行，遽欲釐革，则务学者日以怠惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158384_comment'></div>一旦俾临民政，懵然于其閒，不知治道之所出，犹未能操刀而使之割也，所伤实多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158384_comment'></div>其前项条贯如有闻说未尽事件，欲乞只令有司详定，依旧颁行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158384_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年4月</a>　任监察御史。庆历五年四月丁亥朔，发生日食。作品：论日食。<div id='poem_1158370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158370?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论日食奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158370")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158370_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158370'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158370'>臣伏见四月旦，日当薄蚀，陛下特降德音，亲决庶狱，饬身修政，以应天变，此诚古之圣后明辟克谨天戒之至意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158370_comment'></div>臣闻《汉书》云：「夫至尊莫大乎天，天之变莫大乎日蚀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158370_comment'></div>盖日者，阳之精，人君之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158370_comment'></div>君道亏，为阴所乘，故蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158370_comment'></div>日者，德也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158370_comment'></div>月者，刑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158370_comment'></div>故圣王日蚀修德，月蚀修刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158370_comment'></div>《诗》云：「彼月而食，则惟其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158370_comment'></div>此日而食，于何不臧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158370_comment'></div>说者云：月蚀非常，比之日蚀，固常也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158370_comment'></div>日蚀则不臧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158370_comment'></div>然于正阳之月，法尤忌之，由是有伐鼓用币之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158370_comment'></div>故人君或遭兹变，必避殿彻膳，克己责躬，明君臣，正上下，延纳众议，以辅不逮，如是之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158370_comment'></div>今正阳之月，晻然日蚀，而又亢阳益甚，火灾继作，害孰大焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158370_comment'></div>得非上天有以丁宁垂诫于陛下邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158370_comment'></div>伏望陛下奋乾刚之至德，畏天地之大异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158370_comment'></div>发号施令，审思乎利害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158370_comment'></div>赏德罚罪，无閒于疏昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158370_comment'></div>听断不惑，勤俭为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158370_comment'></div>抑阴尊阳，防微杜渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158370_comment'></div>然后日御便殿，博延公卿，询访直言，讲求古道，励精为治，以答天戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158370_comment'></div>如此，则积异消于上，厉阶绝于下，足以导迎善气，驯致太平，惟陛下留神省察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158370_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　任监察御史。由伴送契丹使返回御史任上，建言选用有才略武臣守边。作品：论边将。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　任监察御史。见河北沿边州郡军粮未备。作品：请添河北入中粮草。<div id='poem_1158525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158525?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请添河北入中粮草奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158525")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158525'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158525'>臣伏读《前汉·赵充国传》，充国尝谓大司农耿寿昌曰：「于金城、湟中籴谷三百万斛，羌人不敢动矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158525_comment'></div>寿昌请籴百万斛，乃得四十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158525_comment'></div>一失此策，羌人故为逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158525_comment'></div>失之毫釐，差之千里，事既然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158525_comment'></div>若四夷猝有动摇，相因而起，虽有智者，不能善其后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158525_comment'></div>是知粮储有备，则边患不足恤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158525_comment'></div>臣窃见河北沿边州郡，军粮未备，屯兵少处，约及二年，如定州屯兵稍众，只及一年有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158525_comment'></div>况中山最是控扼之所，若非次添屯军马，不支数月，缓急如何取济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158525_comment'></div>虽朝廷财用窘迫，力所未及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158525_comment'></div>然河朔根本之地，自黠虏讲好，观衅而动，诡诈万状，固不可信其虚声，怠其实备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158525_comment'></div>《孙子》曰：「无恃其不来，恃吾有以待之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158525_comment'></div>无恃其不攻，恃吾之不可攻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158525_comment'></div>今若计度粮草，处置边事，且循旧制，不务施为，臣恐日甚一日，有不可救之患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158525_comment'></div>故曰：金城汤池，带甲百万，非粟不能守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158525_comment'></div>可不熟虑乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158525_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降指挥，令三司应河北沿边州军，且令依旧入中，若以倍费官钱，即乞支拨见钱百万贯，趁今夏二麦丰熟之际，于近便处及时收籴，却自御河辇运往沿边州军，以实储廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158525_comment'></div>比之贵价入中，其利甚厚，仍乞速赐指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1158525_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　任监察御史。因河北二麦大熟，乞内库尽早支借银绢，收籴诸色斛斗。作品：请河北及时计置斛斗。<div id='poem_1158524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请河北及时计置斛斗奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158524")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158524_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158524'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158524'>臣窃见河北今夏二麦大熟，近朝廷支拨见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158524_comment'></div>及本路应系诸般封桩钱等，并令收籴，共及一百万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158524_comment'></div>逐路粮食虽及年支，亦须接续计置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158524_comment'></div>兼沿边便籴以三说新法，全未有客人入中，已具事由闻奏，乞令沿边且用见钱交钞入中一二年，至今未降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158524_comment'></div>今秋田苗甚好，将来必是丰稔，若不预为擘画，必临时措置不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158524_comment'></div>况积蓄军储，无便于此，时不可失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158524_comment'></div>访闻边郡甚欲得银绢等博籴，或朝廷以三说新行，不欲改法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158524_comment'></div>即望圣慈特许于内库支借银绢一百万匹两，令转运司分配与沿边州军，依见钱价例，收籴诸色斛斗，不惟边储有备，兼免贵价入便，大支却在京钱物等，事体至便。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158524_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　任监察御史。因拯前伴送契丹使，睹迎送三番使臣的费用过大。作品：请止绝三番取索。<div id='poem_1158435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请止绝三番取索奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158435")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158435'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158435'>臣昨奉敕差送伴契丹人使，伏睹三番诸司人依例于接伴使副进发前四五日离京，凡经过驿顿，并先次取索羊面鸡鸭鱼兔之属，广设酒殽，以待两番使臣，所费物料不少，并专副自备供应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158435_comment'></div>及至雄州，动经旬日，本州日供三番下一行使臣等，并散直殿侍长行使臣及手分亲事官酒食约七十馀分，十日之内，纽计甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158435_comment'></div>其馀呼索之物，仍不在数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158435_comment'></div>况常年两次国信使，自有久来体例，过界月日，亦须候接伴使副到雄州，方有过界之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158435_comment'></div>兼接伴使副到本处，尚住三两日，亦足可祗应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158435_comment'></div>臣欲乞特降指挥下国信所，今后三番使臣等，只得于接伴使副前发一日出行，其送伴即先两日分顿，仍只得于当顿排办祗应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158435_comment'></div>如合依衮过驿顿，即不得妄有取索，互以酒食递相管设及馈运，并乞严行止绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158435_comment'></div>兼候送人使过界，即令使副前一日回京，庶沿路州县驿顿易为供给，稍免搔挠官司<span class='inlineComment2'>（《包拯集》卷四。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158435_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1158435'>皇祐二年五月：原无，据《续资治通鉴长编》卷一六八所载事补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158435_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年8月3日</a>　任监察御史。与张郯、何中立考试开封府举人。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0330c2becf10435fa5319515caa640aa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0330c2becf10435fa5319515caa640aa");'><span id='0330c2becf10435fa5319515caa640aa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>，48岁</div><div id='0330c2becf10435fa5319515caa640aa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年春</a>　任监察御史。使契丹还。将启程时，与契丹馆伴论列雄州便门事，使之“但言极是，颇有愧色”。返至雄州，询问此事，归上此疏。作品：奉使契丹辨雄州便门事状。<div id='poem_1158512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉使契丹辨雄州便门事状<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年春）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158512")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158512'>臣等昨于正月初五日离北朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158512_comment'></div>四日夜，正旦馆伴并生辰馆伴与生辰国信使张尧佐、副使张希一及臣等共十人同坐，欲排夜筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158512_comment'></div>方吃茶了，其生辰馆伴副使张宥等先言云：「请暂约退左右，有事要说」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158512_comment'></div>左右既退，张宥等言云：「雄州开东南便门，多纳燕京左右奸细等人，询问北朝事宜，随事大小，各与钱物，此事甚不稳便，请说与雄州」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158512_comment'></div>臣等与张尧佐等即时以理对答且已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158512_comment'></div>相次，张尧佐等依例先退，臣等饮酒，易衣而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158512_comment'></div>至来日，到中路，未坐御筵之前，先令人白馆伴，欲要咨闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158512_comment'></div>相次，馆伴召臣等于厅上，六人同坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158512_comment'></div>臣等说与馆伴云：「昨夕示谕雄州之事，为未知子细，不复款答」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158512_comment'></div>及至饮罢之后，召上节中曾有在雄州指挥者，方子细询问开便门事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158512_comment'></div>其人言：「雄州日近不曾开门，凡有门户，并是旧来开置」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158512_comment'></div>臣等寻语馆伴云：「此事的不足凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158512_comment'></div>设使雄州诱纳奸细，自有正门出入，何必创开一门？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158512_comment'></div>若只是郡中创开门户出入，此亦州郡常事，何关两朝之事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158512_comment'></div>若或北朝燕京及涿州等处开门，本朝岂可言议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158512_comment'></div>兼本朝每戒沿边，不令生事，非不丁宁边臣，岂敢容易？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158512_comment'></div>只如北边臣僚，近年侵入南界，创立城寨，必是北朝不知，知之必不容许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158512_comment'></div>况两朝载言誓书，若欲欢好无穷，莫若遵守盟约，各保疆界」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158512_comment'></div>其馆伴见臣等如此言说，但言极是，颇有愧色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158512_comment'></div>及臣等到雄州，子细询问开门去处，并是李允则已前曾开，后来别无创置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158512_comment'></div>臣等合具奏闻，欲乞密诫雄州，凡有体探事宜，更加慎重，免致漏泄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　任监察御史。主张“无恃其不来，恃吾之不可攻也”作品：论契丹事宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　任监察御史。时任命郭承祐知代州，拯认为不妥，乞将其召回。作品：论边将。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年5月</a>　任监察御史。庆历六年三月，登州地震；五月，京师地震。作品：论地震。<div id='poem_1158371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论地震奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158371")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158371'>臣近闻登州地震山摧，今又镇阳、雄州五月朔日地震，北京、贝州诸处蝗蝻叠生，皆天意先事示变，必不虚发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158371_comment'></div>谨按《汉·五行志》曰：「地之戒莫重于震动」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158371_comment'></div>谓地者阴也，法当安静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158371_comment'></div>今乃越阴之职，专阳之政，其异孰甚焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158371_comment'></div>又夷狄者，中国之阴也，今震于阴长之月，臣恐四夷有谋中国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158371_comment'></div>且雄州控扼北鄙，登州密迩东夷，今继以地震山摧，不可不深思而预备之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158371_comment'></div>顷岁并、代地震，寻以昊贼拒命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158371_comment'></div>近者广南英、连等州亦震，而蛮寇内侵，皆必然已应之兆耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158371_comment'></div>臣近曾上言，沿边将帅尤在得人，乞委执政大臣，精选素习边事之人，以为守将，俾训练卒伍，广为积聚，以大警备之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158371_comment'></div>不然，惧贻陛下之深忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158371_comment'></div>况灾变之作，未有无其应者，惟陛下特留圣意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年春夏间</a>　除任三司户部判官，受赐五品服。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　任三司户部判官。拯批判朝廷大修土木，建议除营房、仓库外，一般寺观祠宇停止修葺。作品：应修造使臣乞依宣命不得乞转官。<div id='poem_1158419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应修造使臣乞依宣命不得乞转官奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158419")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158419'>臣伏见三司修造案，见管营房仓库店宅等共四百馀处，计屋四万馀閒，并系合该修盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158419_comment'></div>今来重建太祖开先殿，虽功用甚大，然王者崇奉之意，诚不可阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158419_comment'></div>所有看池楼、福圣院等，并准传宣权住，窃虑非次别降指挥，依前兴作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158419_comment'></div>缘近年土木之功未尝暂息，材植工匠即日阙乏，兵士劳役，动有咨怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158419_comment'></div>兼逐处并差内臣监修，不以有无准备，立须办集，惟务速毕，以图转官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158419_comment'></div>况国家仓廪未实，财赋有限，费用无极，将何取济！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158419_comment'></div>伏望圣慈省察，候开先殿毕功日，除营房仓廪等合修葺外，应系寺观园苑不急之处，且乞一切权罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158419_comment'></div>兼详景祐二年二月八日宣命节文，应修造了毕，使臣一员、工匠等，并不得乞改转酬奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158419_comment'></div>如显有功绩，即等第与支赐，如违，当行勘断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158419_comment'></div>欲望今后监修使臣等并依宣命指挥，更不得陈乞改转，如有实效，只与支赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年春夏间</a>　任三司户部判官。王逵行事任性，苛政暴敛，非理配率钱物，拯上疏弹劾。作品：弹王逵三章。<div id='poem_1158458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹王逵奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（七　皇祐二年冬）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年春夏间）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158458")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158458'>臣近者与陈旭、吴奎凡六次论列，以新授淮南转运使王逵乞与改授藩郡，至今不蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158458_comment'></div>盖臣等之言不足取信于朝廷如是之甚，俯仰惭惧，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158458_comment'></div>臣今略具王逵逐任事状，伏乞圣慈特赐睿察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158458_comment'></div>按王逵先任湖南转运使日，非理率配数十年役过里正，令纳见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158458_comment'></div>只潭州系七百馀户，虽子孙沦没，及卖过产业者，并令见佃人赔纳，凡干连数千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158458_comment'></div>其部下诸州，率皆类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158458_comment'></div>一路之民，例遭枷锢，逃移死亡者无数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158458_comment'></div>及臣僚论奏，朝廷特与放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158458_comment'></div>又隐匿朝省指挥数月，并不遵禀，一向催纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158458_comment'></div>因事发觉，遂降知池州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158458_comment'></div>其他违越之事，不更条陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158458_comment'></div>故臣僚上言：「伏见王逵凶暴无识，残忍有馀，列位簪绅，心同蛇蝎，因缘奸诈，遂忝职司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158458_comment'></div>在湖南日，酷法诛求财利，茍图进擢，民被杀者，罔知其数」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158458_comment'></div>黜降之后，潭州父老数千人共设大会，以感圣恩，与人去害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158458_comment'></div>在城数万家，三夕香灯彻曙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158458_comment'></div>又被苦之家，并刻木作王逵之形，日夕笞挞，其人心憎恶如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158458_comment'></div>及任江西转运使，依前残酷，枉法徒配民吏，恣行威福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158458_comment'></div>台官举劾，遂下提刑司体量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158458_comment'></div>适属高良夫未到，李道宁移任，王逵权本司公事，乃妄疑前知洪州卞咸到阙说其事迹，遂追捕平民数百人，只于本州倚郭两县收禁，构成卞咸之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158458_comment'></div>况卞咸替罢，将及一年，方行捃拾，以逞私憾，中外莫不扼腕愤嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158458_comment'></div>臣僚继有章疏，遂移荆湖北路，未几复授河东，所为恣横，愈甚于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158458_comment'></div>尝至抚州，筵上与郭志高酒醉诟争，远迩骛骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158458_comment'></div>寻又张圭进状，指论前知福州日在任赃滥不法事件，俱有实状，竟不曾尽理勘劾，止降知光州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158458_comment'></div>据其罪名，不可悉数，虽该赦宥，不可复付以表率之任，且执政大臣，所宜与国家进才良，退苛暴，规恢治体，沮劝将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158458_comment'></div>今乃不恤人言，固用酷吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158458_comment'></div>于一王逵则幸矣，如一路不幸何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158458_comment'></div>臣实为朝廷重惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158458_comment'></div>伏望圣慈令取索前后臣僚奏状，并章珉先勘卞咸狱收坐，及张圭所论之事，同送御史台，依公定夺，即显臣言非妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158458_comment'></div>仍乞检会臣等累进劄子，早赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158458_comment'></div>况杨纮、薛绅、王绰、王鼎，本无残虐之状，只以行事或有过当，尚降差遣，不与牵复职司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158458_comment'></div>较之王逵，彼实非辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158458_comment'></div>臣所以不避烦猥，重此剖述，惟陛下特赐裁处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1158458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　任三司户部判官。杨景宗在任地方官时曾用刑过苛，涂炭生灵。作品：乞不遣杨景宗知磁州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（杨景宗为宋仁宗章惠皇太后的从父弟。）</span><div id='poem_1158406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不遣杨景宗知磁州奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158406")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158406'>臣窃闻观察使杨景宗知磁州，物议喧然，以为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158406_comment'></div>按景宗累经外任，并皆不了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158406_comment'></div>昨自郓州，亦以所为恣横，非次召还，缘禀性不常，用刑过当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158406_comment'></div>今若委之为郡，以亲民政，不惟一州生灵枉被残害，或虑不公事发，须依法施行，恐非所以保全戚属之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158406_comment'></div>其景宗欲望且令依旧与在京差遣，事体至便。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　任三司户部判官。因蔡河上供斛斗数量较定额亏损巨大，拯乞修缮。作品：请修蔡河堰并斗门。<span class='inlineComment2'>（蔡河，一名惠民河。）</span><div id='poem_1158494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请修蔡河堰并斗门奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158494")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158494'>臣前权度支判官日，窃见蔡河每年上供斛斗，系定额六十万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158494_comment'></div>见管三十五纲，自去年以来，般运绝少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158494_comment'></div>庆历五年丙，只般到一十六万二千七百六十七石，比旧额计亏四十三万七千七百三十三石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158494_comment'></div>缘本河所管纲船至多，秋冬行运不绝，盖是催纲使臣等不切用心往来催趁，致此亏欠万数不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158494_comment'></div>兼访闻诸处斗门，例皆破坏，并不修补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158494_comment'></div>其斗门放水，自有时候，多是官员客旅计会不依时候开放，洎纲船及时到彼，即无水可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158494_comment'></div>欲乞下三司指挥，逐县所管斗门，限日近须管疾速牢固添修，不得走透水势，仍令催纲使臣与所辖官员常切提举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158494_comment'></div>如依前曲徇颜情，及信纵公人受倖，不依时候开放，致有邀难住滞，并乞严断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158494_comment'></div>所有纲运，或准前拖延，不及元额，其催纲使臣并乞重行责罚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年夏</a>　任三司户部判官。因向绶迫死太常博士江中立，拯乞对其严惩，以戒将来。作品：乞断向绶二章。<div id='poem_1158427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158427?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞断向绶奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　庆历六年夏）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158427")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158427_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158427'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158427'>臣窃闻太常博士傅莹近沧州制勘回，向绶准前翻变，一行干系九十馀人，依旧收禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158427_comment'></div>窃缘向绶翻变，前后三四次，况證验分明，绝无疑虑，原情至重，坐死犹轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158427_comment'></div>若候具案定罪，必致淹延月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158427_comment'></div>干连人等，盛暑之际，枉被禁系，实可伤悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158427_comment'></div>其向绶，欲望只据累次勘到罪状，特行重断，俾幽冤得伸，狡吏知惧<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158427_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1158427'>庆历六年夏：原无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158427_comment'></div>据《续资治通鉴长编》卷一五八，向绶削官在庆历六年六月，据补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158427_comment'></div>下篇同。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158427_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1158427'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158427_0'>⑴ 《包拯集》卷四。又见《古今图书集成》祥刑典卷一三一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1158427_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1158428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞断向绶奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　庆历六年夏）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158428")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158428'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158428'>臣近者上言，以向绶恐迫通判、太常博士江中立自缢身死，累次勘鞫，拒抗翻变，只乞据前后勘到情款定断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158428_comment'></div>寻于沧州取到案卷，送下法寺，至今多日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158428_comment'></div>窃恐有司执守常制，引用律文，未得允当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158428_comment'></div>况向绶本意，怒中立欲摘发所为不公事件，遂抑勒诸色人等，诬罔陈首中立罪犯，今制勘所又已一一辨明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158428_comment'></div>假中立所犯有状，自有朝廷之法，向绶何得辄用威势凌迫，一至于是，中外无不愤惋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158428_comment'></div>若不特行诛窜，则今后长吏恣为不法，同官僚属稍有言议，即便行捃拾，置于非所，或迫令自尽，或锻成重罪，必无由理雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158428_comment'></div>所系事体甚大，欲望圣慈特于法外重赐裁断，以戒将来。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1158428_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年夏</a>　任三司户部判官。马军副都指挥使许怀德上殿自乞为留后，拯上疏反对，不果。作品：奏许怀德上殿陈乞。<div id='poem_1158418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论许怀德上殿陈乞奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158418")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158418'>臣伏详近降条贯，应系臣僚上殿，不得陈乞恩泽，并令閤门报告，如违，仰御史台弹奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158418_comment'></div>窃见近日臣僚殊不遵禀，例以奏公事为名，因而侥求者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158418_comment'></div>昨兵部郎中马绛差知越州，因上殿叙述乞改官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158418_comment'></div>续又群牧判官吕昌龄自河北牧马回，上殿亦乞省府差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158418_comment'></div>虽各有台谏官论列，然并免勘罚，致今来马军副都指挥使许怀德复上殿乞转观察留后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158418_comment'></div>缘怀德近授观察使，累任别无显效，而不顾邦宪，冒渎圣聪，人之寡廉，一至于是！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158418_comment'></div>欲望特赐取勘施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158418_comment'></div>仍乞今后但是臣僚因奏事陈乞恩理者，或有弹奏，并乞依条勘劾，重行朝典，庶使僭妄之辈稍知警惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158418_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ee4e378080874ec2b6e667a0737cad3f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ee4e378080874ec2b6e667a0737cad3f");'><span id='ee4e378080874ec2b6e667a0737cad3f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1049')">1048-1049年</a>，50-51岁</div><div id='ee4e378080874ec2b6e667a0737cad3f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年6月22日</a>　为三司户部副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年夏</a>　任三司户部副使。乞将同州韩城县的冶铁户除名。作品：请罢同州韩城县铁冶务人户。<div id='poem_1158490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢同州韩城县铁冶务人户奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158490")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158490'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158490'>臣近闻同州韩城县铁冶务，自来定占七百馀户，内二百馀户厚有物力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158490_comment'></div>比见充里正人户，并各高强，只以冶户为名，经今五十馀年，影占州县诸般差役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158490_comment'></div>其冶户内系第一等者，每户逐年供给冶务诸般，所出钱不过三贯文外，更别无所费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158490_comment'></div>况官中所得铁货只及十馀万斤，仍官支买炭并工匠钱三百馀贯，更差专监使臣一员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158490_comment'></div>兼体问得本县人户，以冶务全占却上等力役，及致下等人户差役频并，供应不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158490_comment'></div>若将上件铁数，据等第均在本县人户上，每户约纳官铁，岁不过十斤至二三十斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158490_comment'></div>况本处见卖每斤价钱二十四五文，每户岁纳官铁约费三五百文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158490_comment'></div>虽自来官禁烹炼，彼中私卖甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158490_comment'></div>令百姓取便烹炼，必然铁价转下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158490_comment'></div>兼令赴本县送纳，于民至便，又减省得监官一员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158490_comment'></div>只令本县令佐专管给纳，仍得二百馀户兼充重难役次，颇甚均济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158490_comment'></div>臣在任日，方欲行遣，属以移任，欲乞下本路转运司选差清干官员，往彼相度施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158490_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　任三司户部副使。言凤翔府斜谷造船务等各种苛敛项目，请求免除。作品：请权罢陕西州军科率。<div id='poem_1158480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请权罢陕西州军科率奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158480")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158480'>一、凤翔府斜谷造船务每年造六百料额船六百只，方木物料等，自来分擘与秦、陇、凤翔府诸处采买应付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158480_comment'></div>庆历六年、七年材料等共三十二万，见欠七万有零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158480_comment'></div>庆历八年材料等共二十一万七千有零，全欠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1158480'>一、斜谷务又打造咸阳陕府桥脚船四十四只，合用材料共三万一千有零，见配买次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1158480'>一、修河桩橛共四十五万一千六百五十二条，系七州科买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1158480'>一、上京材木共九万三千一百五条，各系大料木植，十四州科买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1158480'>一、采斫澶州河中府缆索竹一百五十万三千八百二十竿，见差人司竹监斫次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1158480'>一、买上供肉羊兔千口，系十九州军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1158480'>一、买紫草一万斤，系十州军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1158480'>一、买红花四千斤，系六州军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158480_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1158480'>右具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158480_comment'></div>臣勘会凤翔府造船场，每年额船六百只，其方木料，并是本府并陇州量支官钱收买，及于秦州采斫，所差衙前例各赔钱一二千贯，前后人户破荡家产不少，每户锢身者不下三两人，经年未得了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158480_comment'></div>时准三司牒，买修河桩橛四十三万馀条，亦于永兴等七州军配买，比之常岁，多两倍已上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158480_comment'></div>并河中府澶州要缆索竹一百五十万竿，见差人司竹监斫次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158480_comment'></div>今又准三司牒，采买上件材木九万三千条有零，亦是分配永兴等十四州收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158480_comment'></div>缘并系大料木植，只是秦州出产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158480_comment'></div>又闻深入番界，采斫至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158480_comment'></div>其馀不产州军，须至差衙前分买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158480_comment'></div>况陕西州军一年之内三五次，各是大段科配，兼又钱法改更之后，民閒即日大段不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158480_comment'></div>若稍不行宽恤，则疲困之民无保全之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158480_comment'></div>虽详省中书剳子，住九年、十年科买，又只闻说肉羊、紫草、红花之类，并是小可物色，亦易为应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158480_comment'></div>所有逐年买造船场材木物料及桩橛等，最为大害，乞赐详酌指挥，权与蠲免。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1158480_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　任三司户部副使。因江西一路，多以米盐充折绢价，亏损于民，拯乞仁宗查问此事。作品：论江西和买绢。<div id='poem_1158478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论江西和买绢奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158478")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158478'>臣窃闻江南西路今年和买绢价，转运司并以米盐充折，并辖下州军和粜斛斗，多是抑配人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158478_comment'></div>缘本路亦系灾伤地分，民食甚艰，若重有搔扰，必致流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158478_comment'></div>伏睹庆历七年南郊赦文内：「江西一路，多以米盐充折绢价，亏损下民，抑转运司今后须管支见钱和买」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158478_comment'></div>今本路转运司显是故违制旨，专辄施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158478_comment'></div>且命令者，人主之柄，而治乱系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158478_comment'></div>凡朝廷降一命令，所以示信于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158478_comment'></div>若有司承受，委而不顾，乃是命令之不足遵守，俾四方何以取信？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158478_comment'></div>则朝廷纲纪，亦缘此寖隳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158478_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特赐勘问施行，所有斛斗，并令依旧例和籴，不得抑配人户。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年2月</a>　任三司户部副使。皇祐元年二月八日，诏发京师禁军一指挥赴京东西路驻泊以备盗贼。作品：请留禁军不差出招置士兵。<div id='poem_1158499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请留禁军不差出招置土兵奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158499")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158499'>臣闻京师者，天下之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158499_comment'></div>王畿之内，列营屯众，此强本之兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158499_comment'></div>而国家近年以来，边陲有警，乃一例调发，则卫兵日削，恐非固宗社制戎狄之长策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158499_comment'></div>臣以为畿兵虽有大故，不可多调发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158499_comment'></div>前所谓京师者，天下之本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158499_comment'></div>强本者，畿兵耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158499_comment'></div>本固且强，繇中制外，则天下何患焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158499_comment'></div>若调发不已，则耗其财力，而弱其根本，不惟隳祖宗之制，独不念李唐天宝、建中之事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158499_comment'></div>善马精兵，悉出于外，扈卫骁锐，为之一空，卒以重其后害，此朝廷尤宜深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158499_comment'></div>今河北、河东沿边兵寡财匮，卒有急难，惟有民兵可用，往年尝籍之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158499_comment'></div>籍之未甚长策，又从而释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158499_comment'></div>缘河朔之民皆禀气劲悍，义勇奋发，矧又生习边鄙之利害，素谙戎虏之情伪，他路校之不逮远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158499_comment'></div>且向时点阅，舍客取主，又责以户之上下，以是籍之，所得几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158499_comment'></div>窃见唐李抱真民兵之制，事颇相近，故当时昭义一军，雄视山东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158499_comment'></div>将适今之宜，可如抱真之制，约而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158499_comment'></div>不论户下田足田不足，悉以丁力众寡，登降其数而籍之，不及数者，即舍之，取其中稍富实者，令差出谷帛钱货，以给籍丁之贫家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158499_comment'></div>如此，得兵可倍往岁，亦可以少抑兼并，而贫悴之户有所仰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158499_comment'></div>一则供馈不费，二则群情乐为，其处置训练之法，即有祖宗之旧制焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158499_comment'></div>河朔民兵既壮，而禁军留实京师，则内外安矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158499_comment'></div>今北虏诡诈万状，声言西讨，修筑城栅，点集军马，乘此之际，沿边亦宜密令缮完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158499_comment'></div>而议者但恃盟约，殊不设备，万一邀求不已，稍不如意，伺衅而发，曷以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158499_comment'></div>此亦必然之兆，得无熟思乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158499_comment'></div>况边上武将未甚得人，且将者，人之司命，而邦国安危所系，择之不可不审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158499_comment'></div>审将之道，不当限以名位，但辨其能之可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158499_comment'></div>茍得实材，则擢而用之，专而委之，必有成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158499_comment'></div>若不素为之具，缓急旋图之，则无所及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158499_comment'></div>伏望陛下少留圣意，特赐省察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1158499_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　任三司户部副使。仁宗亲制策问。作品：天章阁对策。<div id='poem_1158359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天章阁对策<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年六月至皇祐元年三月间作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158359")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158359'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158359'>问：朕自纂绍庆基，登临御宇，每夕惕以忘劳，虑视听而有怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158359_comment'></div>爰自近岁以来，河朔之閒，民物散亡，水灾流注，甚可哀怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158359_comment'></div>虽已降指挥应灾伤去处并令赈济，及暴露伤损之人各令照管外，其所虑今契丹虽称币，汎使忽来，若非慕化之心，虑有可虞之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158359_comment'></div>复闻聚甲朔边，议收西羌，夙夜经心，深可预防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158359_comment'></div>然事即未萌，诚在安平之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158359_comment'></div>或将来北使诣阙，妄称西去之名，共构衅端，别有邀求之事，诡谲多涂，作何回答？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158359_comment'></div>或以今来诈报西行，傥有南顾之虞，西北山川地形，甚处可为控扼？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158359_comment'></div>今以家国方面之材，且无自荐辅翼之能，实藉众推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158359_comment'></div>傥事有枝梧，帅领何人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158359_comment'></div>洎数路偏将何人可补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158359_comment'></div>欲以威御绥宁，何人堪为镇静？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158359_comment'></div>其朔方自水灾冲破，户口流移，而轸救之外，军储阙乏，财赋屡空，以何法得丰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158359_comment'></div>傥或急速之閒，以何为备？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158359_comment'></div>其向去虽是丰饶，将今所用财货，如何更能省费，致物力以渐从容？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158359_comment'></div>及虑诸路冗兵尚众，作何策精选勇杖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158359_comment'></div>复又战马阙绝，如何敷足？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158359_comment'></div>故事虽未兆，有备无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158359_comment'></div>此系安危，更可询于有位，体朕焦劳，得不周悉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158359_comment'></div>卿等谊在公忠，理当尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158359_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1158359'>臣某昧死再拜言：伏惟陛下有神圣文武之资，绍祖宗大业以驭重柄，三十年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158359_comment'></div>睿谋神断，丰功伟绩，历选明辟，未之前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158359_comment'></div>犹于听政之馀，躬御便坐，笔成圣策，延问近臣，思究当世之切务，兹见陛下降意求治之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158359_comment'></div>臣闻酌言以择善，莫若尽天下之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158359_comment'></div>然万乘之贵，不可使人人毕陈于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158359_comment'></div>故用天下贤豪材杰，参寘近位，就使其中三数人能悉意抗论于赤墀之前，则天下得失之理，如指诸掌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158359_comment'></div>况今广延群论，预谋安危，将相迩臣，博被清问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158359_comment'></div>独臣昏庸无状，将何以奉承诏旨，上副周爰！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158359_comment'></div>谨竭素有一二，条陈以闻，愿陛下以至明择至愚，则臣不胜大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158359_comment'></div>窃以契丹自先朝请盟之后，边鄙无事四十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158359_comment'></div>向以昊贼逆命，因敢上书悖慢，并以和亲割地为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158359_comment'></div>朝廷宽大，未即诛绝，报遣使人，增以金币，又数年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158359_comment'></div>然夷狄之性，不愧贪，不感义，不让胜，不耻败，况内审吾计，有不欲加兵之意乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158359_comment'></div>故自去冬以来，移帐云州，以西讨为名，驻兵未去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158359_comment'></div>今又无故遣使来此，不有邀求，则别生诡计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158359_comment'></div>但虑以不可从之事为言，小不如意，得以为词，解仇协势，启其衅端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158359_comment'></div>何况星文示戒，水灾未弭，天意人事，未甚和顺，惟陛下熟虑而审处之，万一无他，亦不可忽焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158359_comment'></div>况今三路素为控扼之所：中则梁门、遂城，南入镇、定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158359_comment'></div>西则雁门、句注，南入并、代；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158359_comment'></div>东则松亭、石关，南入沧州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158359_comment'></div>然松亭以南数百里，水泽艰险，自北界而出者，则塘水足以限其来路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158359_comment'></div>惟雁门、句注背长城而南，则地里稍广，汉与胡人古今所共出入之路也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1158359_comment'></div>自失山后五镇，此路尤为要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1158359_comment'></div>先朝以骁将杨业守代州，创筑城垒，于今赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1158359_comment'></div>缘代州去云州数程，地又平坦，或有侵轶，此最可虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1158359_comment'></div>孙武曰：「无恃其不来，恃吾有以待之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1158359_comment'></div>无恃其不攻，恃吾之不可攻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1158359_comment'></div>固不可信其虚声，弛其实备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1158359_comment'></div>臣闻将者，人之司命，而邦国安危所系，择之不可不审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1158359_comment'></div>且天下不患乏人，患在不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1158359_comment'></div>用人之道，不必分文武之异，限高卑之差，在其人如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1158359_comment'></div>若得不次进用，则必有成效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1158359_comment'></div>《荀子》曰：「大贤不待次而举，大恶不待次而诛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1158359_comment'></div>谓进退贤不肖，岂须岁月哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1158359_comment'></div>今河北沿边卒骄将惰，粮匮器朽，主兵者非绮纨少年，即罢职老校，隐蔽欺诞，趋过目前，持张皇引惹之说，训练有名无实，闻者可为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1158359_comment'></div>谓宜委中外大臣，精选其有实材者，擢而任之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1158359_comment'></div>其庸懦者，黜而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1158359_comment'></div>若不速为之具，缓急旋图之，则无所及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1158359_comment'></div>且河北者，国家根本之地，存亡系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1158359_comment'></div>近年黄河决溢，水灾尤甚，饥殍过半，公私窘迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1158359_comment'></div>虽累下圣诏，矜恤赈救，使命相望，而农亩荒废，流亡未复，仓廪虚竭，不支数月，此乃前日主中外计者之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1158359_comment'></div>臣顷岁尝奉使送伴，及出疆回日，凡三上言，乞支拨钱帛往河北，当五谷贱时，广谋计置，以备凶荒，终以位疏言贱，不赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1158359_comment'></div>方今粒食翔贵之时，有司虽竭力营办，而财用不足，何以取济！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1158359_comment'></div>若更因循不切措置，恐非社稷之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1158359_comment'></div>惟陛下特出宸断，锐意而遂行之，免成后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1158359_comment'></div>臣尝读《汉书》，宣帝时以西羌未平，京兆尹张敞建议，愿令有罪非盗受财杀人者，皆得以差入谷赎罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1158359_comment'></div>欲乞下有司议，其罪犯可以赎者，条具事件，差入谷多少，俾河北州军得以赎罪，此亦权宜济用之一端尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1158359_comment'></div>兼三路官员甚众，伏见真宗皇帝朝以河北荒歉，减省京朝官、使臣、幕职等七十五员，其逐路部署押阵使军职，自观察而下，悉罢赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1158359_comment'></div>此先朝令典，愿陛下遵而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1158359_comment'></div>臣又闻河北屯兵无虑三十馀万，然备边防，严武事，不可阙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1158359_comment'></div>而老弱者众，缓急又不可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1158359_comment'></div>当此艰食之际，供费寖广，万一粮储不继，势必生变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1158359_comment'></div>望令本路转运、安抚司拣退老病冗弱，以宽物力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1158359_comment'></div>且老弱去，则精锐者勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1158359_comment'></div>物力宽，则赡养者足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1158359_comment'></div>其近里兵伍，即令渐次抽那于有粮储州军就食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1158359_comment'></div>不然，则物力俱竭，为患不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1158359_comment'></div>臣又见顷岁于郓、同州置二马监，各侵占民田数千顷，乃于河北监内分马往逐处牧养，未逾一月，死者十有七八，迄今为二州之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1158359_comment'></div>议者谓不若依旧尽归河北诸监，以其地给民，则马无所损，民得其利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1158359_comment'></div>缘马监直属群牧司，逐州官吏不得统辖，利害无由而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1158359_comment'></div>今若委转运使兼领，则巡按察视，可以革去积弊，岁继月及，必至增羡，又何患战马不足哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1158359_comment'></div>臣前所条陈，皆国家之常务，而言事者多及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1158359_comment'></div>臣谓今之切务者，在择政府大臣敢当天下之责，独立不惧，而以安危为己任者，委以经制四方，庶几可弭向者之患，而纾陛下之忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1158359_comment'></div>臣愚以为言之者不难，事行则为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1158359_comment'></div>古人有云：「言之必可行也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1158359_comment'></div>又曰：「知之非艰，行之惟艰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1158359_comment'></div>愿陛下参举众善，事符机会者，思而行之，则千虑一得，庶少补于睿聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1158359_comment'></div>辞浅气索，惟陛下裁察，幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_86_1158359_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='17daebdfe297456b9e064cabc4e0d082_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("17daebdfe297456b9e064cabc4e0d082");'><span id='17daebdfe297456b9e064cabc4e0d082_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1052')">1049-1052年</a>，51-54岁</div><div id='17daebdfe297456b9e064cabc4e0d082' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　任三司户部副使。奉使陕西还。作品：请除范祥陕西转运副使。<div id='poem_1158398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请除范祥陕西转运副使奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158398")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158398'>臣伏见近降敕命，「陕西盐法且依范祥擘画，通商放行」，此诚国家大利便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158398_comment'></div>而中外臣僚不详末本，时有横议，所赖朝廷特与主张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158398_comment'></div>兼范祥见充本路提点刑狱，与转运司每常公事往来，或至违异，必恐不能协心以济，深属不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158398_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特许就除范祥权本路转运副使，只理提点刑狱资序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158398_comment'></div>所贵擘画盐法利害，计置沿边斛斗，事归一局，易为办集。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　任三司户部副使。针对当时冗官、冗兵等现象，建言减冗杂而节用度。作品：论冗官财用等。<div id='poem_1158368' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158368' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158368?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论冗官财用等奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158368")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158368_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158368'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158368'>臣伏见景德、祥符中，文武官总九千七百八十五员；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158368_comment'></div>今内外官属总一万七千三百馀员，其未授差遣京官使臣及守选人不在数内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158368_comment'></div>较之先朝，才四十馀年，已逾一倍多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158368_comment'></div>窃以唐、虞建官惟百，夏、商倍之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158368_comment'></div>周设六官，僚属渐广；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158368_comment'></div>秦并六国，郡县益众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158368_comment'></div>降及汉、魏，以至隋、唐，虽设官寖多，然未有如本朝繁冗之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158368_comment'></div>今天下州郡三百二十，县一千二百五十，而一州一县所任之职，素有定额，大率用吏不过五六千员则有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158368_comment'></div>今乃三倍其多，而又三岁一开贡举，每放仅千人，复有台寺之小吏，府监之杂工，荫序之官，进纳之辈，总而计之，不止于三倍，是食禄者日增，力田者日耗，则国计民力安得不窘乏哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158368_comment'></div>臣谨按景德中，天下财赋等岁入四千七百二十一万一千匹贯石两，支四千九百七十四万八千九百匹贯石两；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158368_comment'></div>在京岁入一千八百三十九万二千匹贯石两，支一千五百四十万四千九百匹贯石两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158368_comment'></div>庆历八年，天下财赋等岁入一万三百五十九万六千四百匹贯石两，支八千九百三十八万三千七百匹贯石两；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158368_comment'></div>在京岁入一千八百九十九万六千五百匹贯石两，支二千二百四十万九百匹贯石两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158368_comment'></div>况天下税籍有常数矣，今则岁入倍多者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158368_comment'></div>盖祖宗之世，所输之税只纳本色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158368_comment'></div>自后以用度日广，所纳并从折变，重率暴敛，日甚一日，何穷之有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158368_comment'></div>且天下田土财用，比之曩时，虚耗渐以不逮，岂于今而能倍之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158368_comment'></div>非天降地出，但诛求于民无纪极尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158368_comment'></div>输者已竭，取者未足，则大本安所固哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158368_comment'></div>臣以为冗吏耗于上，冗兵耗于下，欲救其弊，当治其源，在乎减冗杂而节用度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158368_comment'></div>若冗杂不减，用度不节，虽善为计，亦不能救也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158368_comment'></div>方今山泽之利竭矣，征赋之入尽矣，幸而西北无事，乃是可为之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158368_comment'></div>若不锐意而改图，但务因循，必恐贻患将来，有不可救之过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158368_comment'></div>伏望上体祖宗之成宪，下恤生灵之重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158368_comment'></div>谓设官太多也，则宜艰难选举，澄汰冗杂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158368_comment'></div>谓养兵太众也，则宜罢绝招募，拣斥老弱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158368_comment'></div>土木之工不急者悉罢之，科率之出无名者并除之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158368_comment'></div>省禁中奢侈之僭，节上下浮枉之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158368_comment'></div>当承平之代，建长久之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158368_comment'></div>愿陛下留神省察，申命宰执，条此数事而力行之，则天下幸甚。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1158368'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1158368_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　任三司户部副使。建言“薄赋敛，宽力役，救饥馑”，以赠民户。作品：论历代并本朝户口。<div id='poem_1158466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论历代并本朝户口奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐二年作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158466")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158466'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158466'>臣近者获登云陛，亲奉德音，询及本朝并唐编户多少之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158466_comment'></div>臣虽粗陈梗槩，不足以上对清问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158466_comment'></div>退而遍考诸史，尽见历代本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158466_comment'></div>窃以三代虽盛，其户口记籍莫得而详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158466_comment'></div>国史所起，惟两汉最备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158466_comment'></div>谨按前汉元始二年，人户千二百二十三万三千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158466_comment'></div>及后汉光武兵革渐息之后，户四百二十七万六百三十，永寿二年增至一千六十七万九百六十：此两汉极盛之数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158466_comment'></div>三国鼎峙，干戈日寻，版籍岁减，当时才百四十馀万耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158466_comment'></div>晋自武帝平吴之后，编户二百四十五万九千八百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158466_comment'></div>自后南北幅裂，户无常数，少者不盈百万，多者不过三倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158466_comment'></div>隋文帝平一天下，至大业二年，户八百九十万七千五百三十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158466_comment'></div>及乎唐之初年，人户不满三百万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158466_comment'></div>至高宗永徽元年，渐增至三百八十万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158466_comment'></div>明皇天宝十三载已前，最为全盛，只及九百六万九千一百五十四；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158466_comment'></div>自安史构乱之后，屠戮生灵几尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158466_comment'></div>乾元已后，仅满一百至二百万耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158466_comment'></div>至武宗会昌年中，其閒相距百馀岁，才增至四百九十五万五千一百五十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158466_comment'></div>降及五代，战伐相蹂，日益耗散，是时四分窃据之地，逐处户口各有数十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158466_comment'></div>太祖皇帝建隆之初，有户九十六万七千三百五十三，自后取剑南，平岭表，下江左，辟湖湘，所得户口方逾百万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158466_comment'></div>至开宝九年，渐加至三百九万五百四户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158466_comment'></div>太宗皇帝至道二年，已增至四百五十一万四千二百五十七；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158466_comment'></div>真宗皇帝天禧五年，又增至八百六十七万七千六百七十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158466_comment'></div>陛下御宇已来，与民休息，至天圣七年，凡计编户一千一十六万二千六百八十九；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158466_comment'></div>至庆历二年，增至一千三十万七千六百四十八户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158466_comment'></div>八年又增至一千九十六万四千四百三十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158466_comment'></div>臣以谓前代户口之目，三代已降，跨唐越汉，未有若今之盛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158466_comment'></div>臣闻蚩蚩生聚，蕃息衰耗，一出于时政之所陶化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158466_comment'></div>是故明主知其然也，则必薄赋敛，宽力役，救荒馑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158466_comment'></div>三者不失，然后幼有所养，老有所终，无夭阏之伤，无庸调之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158466_comment'></div>此乃陛下日慎一日，以致其盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158466_comment'></div>若遂与之休养，则可封之俗，不异二帝之世矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1158466_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年春</a>　擢为天章阁待制、知谏院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。举荐孙甫、孙环二人。作品：请召还孙甫张环。<div id='poem_1158394' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158394' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158394?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请召还孙甫张环奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158394")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158394'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158394'>臣近蒙圣恩，擢预谏职，固让则有嫌疑之避，轻受则有忝冒之愧，进退失措，罔知宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158394_comment'></div>伏况谏垣之才，方今极选，用人之得失，系国之轻重，固不可不慎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158394_comment'></div>臣窃见起居舍人、秘阁校理孙甫，兵部员外郎、秘阁校理张环，禀纯一之性，有端方之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158394_comment'></div>危言笃论，可以正阙遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158394_comment'></div>博学远识，可以备顾问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158394_comment'></div>欲乞特与召还，置之近列，则言路益广，公议允协。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1158394_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。庶人冷青诈称皇子，拯与赵概奉旨查办冷青公事。作品：论妖人冷青等事二章。<div id='poem_1158437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论妖人冷清等事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　皇祐二年春）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158437")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158437'>臣奉敕差与赵槩等录问冷清公事，臣寻往军巡院将公案看详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158437_comment'></div>据冷清款招伏，前后狂言非一，原其情状，法所无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158437_comment'></div>致之极典，固在不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158437_comment'></div>兼详放停军人高继安款，先因罪犯配鼎州，寻隙入京，托病放免，而妄谈幻术，交结权贵，所至之处，多以祷祠为名，扇惑州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158437_comment'></div>顷年于潭州即将带冷清随行，沿路累造妖言，知而故纵，不以告官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158437_comment'></div>及冷清事发，则教令诈作心风，果得免罪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158437_comment'></div>寻又教以狂悖之语，所不忍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158437_comment'></div>且都城之内，岂可令此辈轻慢宪法，惑乱大众？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158437_comment'></div>若不速行显戮，以戒未来，则启奸邪之心，为国生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158437_comment'></div>防微杜渐，不可忽也，乞令尽法施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158437_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论妖人冷清等事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　皇祐二年春）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158438")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158438'>臣近以开封府勘到冷清、高继安等，乞早行显戮，免惑中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158438_comment'></div>况狂伪之状，灼然明白，决无可疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158438_comment'></div>天地所不容，人神所共弃，岂宜引用常法，迁延不断？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158438_comment'></div>此而可忍，孰不可恕！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158438_comment'></div>兼风霾暴作，日色无光，上下蒙蔽之象，故天示此变，所以警悟人君如是之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158438_comment'></div>伏愿陛下察变异之来，顾宗社之重，特出宸断，速令诛夷，免奸邪之类别起衅端，寖成大患。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1158438_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年5月</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。从包拯等建议，罢三番使臣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年6月</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。与陈旭、吴奎等上疏弹劾张尧佐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年夏秋间</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。建言当宽养黎庶，固其大本，使四方之民享皇帝之恩泽。作品：论赦恩不及下。<div id='poem_1158366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158366?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论赦恩不及下奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐二年作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年夏秋间）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158366")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158366'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158366'>臣伏闻先帝时，冬十二月雷震，司天监奏主国家发惠布泽未及黎庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158366_comment'></div>上召辅臣谓之曰：「此上天所以警朕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158366_comment'></div>且河北、关西戍兵未息，民人劳止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158366_comment'></div>又三司转运使率扰之事，名类实繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158366_comment'></div>大者宜即减省，小者悉蠲除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158366_comment'></div>将来改元赦书，卿等宜尽采民弊，著为条目，务泽及黎庶也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158366_comment'></div>大哉，先帝爱民之心如是之至！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158366_comment'></div>以陛下求治之心，亦先帝之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158366_comment'></div>臣切见陕西用兵之后，朝廷急于馈运，多所经画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158366_comment'></div>丁夫征赋有常数矣，若踰之，则尽为无名之率；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158366_comment'></div>其他酒税钱谷之类亦有定额矣，而贪于宠利者，惟务聚敛，掊克于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158366_comment'></div>前后刻暴，竞以相胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158366_comment'></div>前者增几十万，以图厚赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158366_comment'></div>后者则又增几十万，以图优赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158366_comment'></div>日甚一日，何穷之有，而民力困且竭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158366_comment'></div>所以疮痏天下，于今未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158366_comment'></div>用是观之，其实岂为国乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158366_comment'></div>果为国，岂不以爱民为心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158366_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「与其有聚敛之臣，宁有盗臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158366_comment'></div>则先王顾生民何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158366_comment'></div>今虽用度微窘，而诸州旱潦相继，亦当宽养黎庶，固其大本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158366_comment'></div>大本不固，则国家从何而安哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158366_comment'></div>况朝廷比下诏令，未尝不以宽民恤物为先，而有司往往不即遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158366_comment'></div>是陛下有忧民之心，而民无繇知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158366_comment'></div>使王泽壅于上，民情郁于下，此皆向者有司之失，恐非所以流布恺悌，慰安元元之深旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158366_comment'></div>臣欲乞应自西事以来一切权宜之事，因循未釐革者，将来明堂赦书，尽采馀弊，著之条目，悉与改正，以为定制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158366_comment'></div>若民閒夏秋二税，除依例输纳外，不得非横支移折变，茶盐酒税课利，一切依旧额趁办，勿许擅有增减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158366_comment'></div>诸色欠负，自来每遇恩贷，不以存亡，必根究本末，但务追摄，罕得除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158366_comment'></div>乞令今后于理合该蠲免者，更不缧系逮捕，重为烦扰，并令疾速检会除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158366_comment'></div>若有司稽违，必严行黜责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158366_comment'></div>如此，则上可以遵先帝之意，下可以救当世之愚，俾四方之人知陛下旷荡之泽实及于下，则海内幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1158366_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年8月</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。建言止绝内降。作品：请绝内降。<div id='poem_1158413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158413?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请绝内降奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（为天章阁待制知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158413")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158413_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158413'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158413'>臣窃见天圣中凡有内降，莫测夤缘，尽由请托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158413_comment'></div>盖倾邪之辈，因左右之容，假援中闱，久渎圣化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158413_comment'></div>洎陛下亲览庶政，首革兹弊，侥荣滥赏，人不能以倖求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158413_comment'></div>顷年以来，此路寖启，妨公害政，无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158413_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后应中外之人阴有交结，或冒陈劳效，以图荣宠，或比缘罪犯，茍希横贷，伏望圣慈特降指挥止绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158413_comment'></div>如更妄有陈乞，并今中书、枢密院、三司、开封府等处详先降指挥，依公执奏，毋得阿徇，上累圣明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1158413_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。时郭承祐改差许州，虽罢知州，仍为节度使。拯再次弹劾。作品：弹郭承祐二章。<div id='poem_1158447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹郭承祐奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　皇祐二年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158447")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158447'>臣等近曾再具论列郭承祐，以其上僭不法等事，乞朝廷重行降黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158447_comment'></div>今闻改差许州部署，虽罢知州之权，然依前为节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158447_comment'></div>在承祐所损无几，于朝廷威令则所损至重至深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158447_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158447_comment'></div>承祐以亲以旧，曲被优恩，有大罪而蒙生全，无微功而叨将领，便蕃富贵，出入宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158447_comment'></div>假使杀身，未能报德，而乃恣逞奸慝，渎乱国经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158447_comment'></div>身拥节旄，而姑息士卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158447_comment'></div>职邻枢近，而僭越典常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158447_comment'></div>命之抚俗而残民，委之留务而生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158447_comment'></div>喧然众口，谓之蓄谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158447_comment'></div>迹其用心，实亦不顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158447_comment'></div>此而可恕，则天下之恶无不可容者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158447_comment'></div>虽人主曲全臣下，过示优矜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158447_comment'></div>而凶人不顾君亲，胡为惕厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158447_comment'></div>况当熙洽之际，敢萌跋扈之为，是诱藩臣，非曰戎首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158447_comment'></div>若不痛绳以法，斯则漏彼吞舟，使包藏祸乱之人，何以戒惧而自戢哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158447_comment'></div>兼臣等仍闻承祐在南京，非理决配过人及一二百数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158447_comment'></div>昨杨孜分析，才四十五人而已，实有未尽，意其谓何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158447_comment'></div>臣等乞再下南京，令子细分析承祐在任日决配过军人百姓，依法不依法，作两项声说的实数目闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158447_comment'></div>候文字到日，乞朝廷别赐裁处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1158447_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹郭承祐奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　皇祐二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158448")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158448'>臣等已三次论列郭承祐，乞朝廷据其迹状，重行降黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158448_comment'></div>至今未奉俞旨，臣等实以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158448_comment'></div>然所忧者，非谓以言未从及身计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158448_comment'></div>诚忧国家威令不行，则凶人无以戒惧，开奸宄之隙，发贼乱之萌，贻戚将来，固不细也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158448_comment'></div>圣人思患预防，君子见几而作，皆慎于微小，则其祸易除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158448_comment'></div>及事变之后，虽有智谋，即能戡定，所伤亦已多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158448_comment'></div>承祐猖獗，奚足顾忌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158448_comment'></div>但因之生事，则祸亦不轻，臣等所以区区不能自止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158448_comment'></div>传曰：「除君之恶，惟力是视」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158448_comment'></div>臣等虽其力微，不能感动天听，以摧压横猾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158448_comment'></div>至若自爱其身，遇事面从，则不忍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158448_comment'></div>陛下何惜一倖臣，不正其罪，使威令行，朝廷肃，明示四方之臣庶邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158448_comment'></div>臣等实甚惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158448_comment'></div>伏乞检会前来劄子，必赐施行，无任恳激之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年9月</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。明堂大赦前，拯上疏乞严惩贪官，纵遇大赦，不可复以官爵。作品：请赃吏该恩未得叙用。<div id='poem_1158430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请赃吏该恩未得叙用奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158430")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158430'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158430'>臣窃闻太宗朝，臣僚或犯赃罪，并配少府监隶役，及该赦宥，谓近臣曰：「此既犯赃污，只可放令逐便，不可复以官爵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158430_comment'></div>其责贪残、慎名器也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158430_comment'></div>且两汉以赃私致罪者，尚禁锢子孙，矧自犯之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158430_comment'></div>今明堂大赦，应系贬降臣僚，例该录用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158430_comment'></div>若张可久，先任淮南转运使日，以自贩私盐、剩收职田黜削，累经叙用，已任蔡州节度副使，见监陈州粮料，今来不可更复正官，欲望且与散官量移差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158430_comment'></div>其馀应以赃滥致罪者，乞不一例录用，所贵赃吏稍知警惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1158430_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年10月</a>　任天章阁待制、知谏院。仁宗皇祐二年九月二十七日，明堂“大赦，百官进秩一等”作品：论明堂覃恩。<div id='poem_1158414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论明堂覃恩奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐二年知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158414")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158414'>臣伏睹明堂敕书，应文武百官内臣并与迁转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158414_comment'></div>臣先以风闻，曾具论列，并乞召对，不蒙开可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158414_comment'></div>退用忧迫，弗皇启处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158414_comment'></div>窃以爵禄者，天下之公器，而邦国之大柄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158414_comment'></div>惟士之有功与德，所宜处之，非此二者，不可滥与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158414_comment'></div>夫人君者，固宜慎之惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158414_comment'></div>苟轻用之，则坏公器而失大柄，一纲或紊，百目皆隳，虽善为治者，亦末如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158414_comment'></div>况今吏员益众，财用益殚，为国计者，自当澄汰冗杂，以宽调度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158414_comment'></div>岂可不辨能否，普加官爵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158414_comment'></div>是于承平之世，行此姑息之事，但恐赋租之广不足供其用，秩廪之多不足充其欲，纪律一弛，天下荡然，有不可救之弊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158414_comment'></div>臣又伏读近降诏旨，今后应内降特与恩泽，及免减罪犯，并仰中书、枢密院并所承受官司具前后诏敕执奏，不得施行，有以见陛下厉精革弊求治之切至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158414_comment'></div>惟此覃恩，颇蠹政之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158414_comment'></div>伏望陛下上禀祖宗之训，下为社稷之计，所有今来迁转恩泽，乞赐特行裁处，免千古之下，以累圣德之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158414_comment'></div>臣过叨宠擢，位疏责重，区区之恳，不能自已，惟陛下留神省察，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　以明堂恩，官迁兵部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年10月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。建言放免民户欠负的赋税。作品：论放欠。<span class='inlineComment2'>（次月五日，拯便奉诏“放天下欠负”）</span><div id='poem_1158479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论放欠奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐二年知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158479")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158479'>臣伏睹明堂赦书，应今日以前天下欠负官物，并于干系保人名下催纳，元非侵欺盗用，或虽是侵盗，见今本家并干系保人内委无抵当者，并令本属及转运司保明闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158479_comment'></div>其累经官吏保明，三司未与除放者，限赦到一月内，令本处先具自来保明度数，申本路转运司疾速保明，缴连闻奏，当议并与除放，此诚陛下优恤元元如是之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158479_comment'></div>然臣历观前后赦文，凡所恩贷，无不周悉，而有司往往废格不即遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158479_comment'></div>臣窃闻真宗咸平年中，亲御便殿，放三司所引诸色违欠，凡四千一百六人，计物八万三千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158479_comment'></div>盖先帝以恩诏每宥逋责，有司必究问本末，或缧系追逮，益为烦扰，故命以籍引对而面释之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158479_comment'></div>大哉先帝，忧民轸物之心，惟恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158479_comment'></div>伏望陛下特降指挥，委三司将应系诸色逋欠人，各具因依，一一类聚，备录申奏，并令引见，详酌除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158479_comment'></div>如此，则恩出于上，弊绝于下矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。拯言时财用窘迫，宜精选三司使、转运使等计臣。作品：请选内外计臣二章。<div id='poem_1158407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选内外计臣奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　皇祐二年九月知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158407")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158407'>臣窃见天下财用，积年窘乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158407_comment'></div>近自明堂礼毕，赏赉才罢，又行特给，支费浩瀚，帑藏虚竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158407_comment'></div>且朝廷所仰给者，江淮、两浙，逐路旱涝相继，兼又茶法隳坏，商算不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158407_comment'></div>东南州军，钱帛粮斛自不足用，则四方岁入之数，所得几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158407_comment'></div>今之总邦计者，内则三司使，外则转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158407_comment'></div>当此财用窘乏之际，居职者尤宜佥求才杰之士，俾之兴利除害，庶几可济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158407_comment'></div>若乃上下循默，恬然以为无事，不务更张措置，必恐日甚一日，有不可救之患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158407_comment'></div>伏望圣慈申命有司，以今之一岁出入，较近年用度，耗登之数则断可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158407_comment'></div>所有内外总计之臣，欲乞特出宸断，精加推择，选任能者，责以实效，庶免将来败事，惟陛下留神省察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158407_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选内外计臣奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　皇祐二年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158408")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158408'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158408'>臣近以天下财用，公私窘乏，而主计之吏，近则三司使，外则转运使，乞精加选擢，委任能者，免致将来败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158408_comment'></div>兼吴奎、陈旭等累曾论列，终未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158408_comment'></div>窃缘三司使张尧佐早缘恩倖，骤阶华要，任之会府，委以大计，而本职隳废，利权反覆，公私困敝，中外危惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158408_comment'></div>且历代后妃之族，虽有才者，亦未尝假以事权，又况庸庸不才者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158408_comment'></div>但富贵保全之，则无害矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158408_comment'></div>臣伏见国朝自祖宗以来，当帑廪丰盈，用度充足之际，尚乃精选计臣如陈恕、魏羽等辈用之，其馀亦尽一时之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158408_comment'></div>况今上下窘迫如是，岂可专任此人，久居是职哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158408_comment'></div>失天下之望，误天下之事，臣实为陛下痛惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158408_comment'></div>伏望特出宸断，授尧佐以他职，别求才杰之士，委而任之，责以实效，一二年閒，庶几可济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158408_comment'></div>不然，惧贻陛下之深忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158408_comment'></div>且宗社至重，财用至急，而安危系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158408_comment'></div>惟陛下特留圣意，臣无任激切恳迫之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158408_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年11月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。奉诏放天下欠负。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。十月，王逵移任淮南转运使，拯多次上疏言其不当为此重任。作品：弹王逵四章。<div id='poem_1158458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹王逵奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（七　皇祐二年冬）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年春夏间）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158458")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158458'>臣近者与陈旭、吴奎凡六次论列，以新授淮南转运使王逵乞与改授藩郡，至今不蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158458_comment'></div>盖臣等之言不足取信于朝廷如是之甚，俯仰惭惧，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158458_comment'></div>臣今略具王逵逐任事状，伏乞圣慈特赐睿察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158458_comment'></div>按王逵先任湖南转运使日，非理率配数十年役过里正，令纳见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158458_comment'></div>只潭州系七百馀户，虽子孙沦没，及卖过产业者，并令见佃人赔纳，凡干连数千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158458_comment'></div>其部下诸州，率皆类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158458_comment'></div>一路之民，例遭枷锢，逃移死亡者无数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158458_comment'></div>及臣僚论奏，朝廷特与放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158458_comment'></div>又隐匿朝省指挥数月，并不遵禀，一向催纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158458_comment'></div>因事发觉，遂降知池州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158458_comment'></div>其他违越之事，不更条陈。<div class='inline'
