id='poem_sentence_10_1158458_comment'></div>故臣僚上言：「伏见王逵凶暴无识，残忍有馀，列位簪绅，心同蛇蝎，因缘奸诈，遂忝职司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158458_comment'></div>在湖南日，酷法诛求财利，茍图进擢，民被杀者，罔知其数」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158458_comment'></div>黜降之后，潭州父老数千人共设大会，以感圣恩，与人去害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158458_comment'></div>在城数万家，三夕香灯彻曙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158458_comment'></div>又被苦之家，并刻木作王逵之形，日夕笞挞，其人心憎恶如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158458_comment'></div>及任江西转运使，依前残酷，枉法徒配民吏，恣行威福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158458_comment'></div>台官举劾，遂下提刑司体量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158458_comment'></div>适属高良夫未到，李道宁移任，王逵权本司公事，乃妄疑前知洪州卞咸到阙说其事迹，遂追捕平民数百人，只于本州倚郭两县收禁，构成卞咸之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158458_comment'></div>况卞咸替罢，将及一年，方行捃拾，以逞私憾，中外莫不扼腕愤嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158458_comment'></div>臣僚继有章疏，遂移荆湖北路，未几复授河东，所为恣横，愈甚于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158458_comment'></div>尝至抚州，筵上与郭志高酒醉诟争，远迩骛骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158458_comment'></div>寻又张圭进状，指论前知福州日在任赃滥不法事件，俱有实状，竟不曾尽理勘劾，止降知光州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158458_comment'></div>据其罪名，不可悉数，虽该赦宥，不可复付以表率之任，且执政大臣，所宜与国家进才良，退苛暴，规恢治体，沮劝将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158458_comment'></div>今乃不恤人言，固用酷吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158458_comment'></div>于一王逵则幸矣，如一路不幸何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158458_comment'></div>臣实为朝廷重惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158458_comment'></div>伏望圣慈令取索前后臣僚奏状，并章珉先勘卞咸狱收坐，及张圭所论之事，同送御史台，依公定夺，即显臣言非妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158458_comment'></div>仍乞检会臣等累进劄子，早赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158458_comment'></div>况杨纮、薛绅、王绰、王鼎，本无残虐之状，只以行事或有过当，尚降差遣，不与牵复职司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158458_comment'></div>较之王逵，彼实非辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158458_comment'></div>臣所以不避烦猥，重此剖述，惟陛下特赐裁处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1158458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年闰11月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。张尧佐骤除宣徽南院使、淮康军节度使、景灵宫使、群牧制置四使。拯乞罢其宣徽使之命任以外镇。作品：弹张尧佐。<span class='inlineComment2'>（张尧佐为仁宗宠妃张贵妃从父。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。复上疏论张尧佐除四使不当。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。建言任命官员时斥去形迹之弊，广开公正之路。作品：论大臣形迹事。<div id='poem_1158364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论大臣形迹事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158364")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158364'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158364'>臣伏见朝廷累年以来，凡进用庶官，裁处大事，必避形迹，以为公道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158364_comment'></div>上下相蔽，习以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158364_comment'></div>有才者以形迹而不敢用，不才者以形迹而不敢去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158364_comment'></div>事有可为者以形迹而不为，事有不可行者以形迹而或行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158364_comment'></div>此盖苟避中伤，以防后害尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158364_comment'></div>为身谋则可，为国谋则不当如是，此最时政之大害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158364_comment'></div>且天子择宰相，宰相择诸司官长，诸司官长参举僚属，俾公卿大夫而下，各称其职，然后推诚委任，坦无疑贰，则中外协济，政务脩举，如此而不臻古治者，臣所未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158364_comment'></div>臣伏读《唐书》，太宗朝或言魏徵阿党者，帝使温彦博验之，无状，因令彦博让之，且曰：「今后不得不存形迹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158364_comment'></div>他日，徵入奏，曰：「臣闻君臣协契，义同一体，岂可不存公道，惟事形迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158364_comment'></div>若君臣上下同遵此路，则邦之兴丧或未可知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158364_comment'></div>帝瞿然改容曰：「吾已悔之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158364_comment'></div>又高宗尝责侍臣不进贤才，李安期对曰：「圣帝明王，莫不劳于求贤，逸于任使，设使尧、舜苦己癯瘠，不能用贤，亦王化不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158364_comment'></div>况天下至广，非无英彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158364_comment'></div>但比近公卿荐引，即遭嚣谤，以为朋党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158364_comment'></div>况沈滞者未伸，而在位者已损，所以人思茍免，竞为缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158364_comment'></div>若人主虚己招纳，广务搜访，不忌恩雠，惟能是用，谗既不入，谁敢不竭忠诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158364_comment'></div>此皆事由君上，非臣下所能致也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158364_comment'></div>高宗深纳其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158364_comment'></div>所以贞观、永徽之代，最号太平者，盖由广延纳之道，推至公之心，使之然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158364_comment'></div>宜乎载在史册，焕为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158364_comment'></div>伏自陛下嗣守神器，已逾二纪，日御便殿，孜孜求治，虽古先哲王，未有如是之焦劳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158364_comment'></div>而时多疵疠，民未富庶，国廪罕蓄，邦计益削者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158364_comment'></div>盖知人用人之道恐有所未尽尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158364_comment'></div>昔齐桓公问管仲曰：「何者害霸」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158364_comment'></div>曰：「不能知人，害霸也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158364_comment'></div>知而不能用，害霸也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158364_comment'></div>用而不能信，害霸也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158364_comment'></div>既信而又使小人参之，害霸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158364_comment'></div>夫管仲一诸侯佐尔，犹慎于信用小人，况巍巍盛德，复将有所閒然乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158364_comment'></div>伏望陛下奋乾刚之威，确然英断，申命宰执进用贤俊，斥去形迹之弊，以广公正之路，判忠佞，抑侥倖，察左右爱憎之说，延中外谠直之议，慎重名器，振举纲目，则可使教惇于上，民悦于下，召天地之和气，致邦国于永宁，惟在陛下日慎一日，力行而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1158364_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。主张制定新的茶法，减轻茶税。作品：论茶法二章。<div id='poem_1158495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论茶法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　皇祐二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158495")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158495'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158495'>臣窃见国朝茶利课额，自收复江浙之后，总山场榷货务，逐岁共得钱四百馀万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158495_comment'></div>太平兴国之初，并是实钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158495_comment'></div>其后西北边急，于刍粟入中，遂添估耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158495_comment'></div>江淮出茶之所，西北入粟之地，不相应会，以是实值尽为虚钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158495_comment'></div>至大中祥符六年、七年，亦各及三百万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158495_comment'></div>末年虽不及元额，在京榷货务尚得引钱一百五十万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158495_comment'></div>自顷年变法以来，惟存虚额，其实入之数益少，近岁尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158495_comment'></div>访闻去年江淮共亏一百三十万贯，即未知在京榷物务所亏数目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158495_comment'></div>昨准敕节文，三司奏，据榷货务擘画，以河北客人入纳及配率斛斗，给过三色交钞，内茶交钞每一百贯文贴纳三十四贯，支与一百贯茶货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158495_comment'></div>近又准敕命，应买下庆历五年分茶钞，减十五贯，每一百贯只贴纳十九贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158495_comment'></div>其皇祐元年茶钞，依旧贴纳三十四贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158495_comment'></div>缘客人百姓等，于河北入纳，给得交钞到京，每一百贯只直三四十贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158495_comment'></div>今虽量与减数，亦是与配率无异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158495_comment'></div>而欲望客旅兴贩，及招诱入官，其可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158495_comment'></div>近盐铁副使仲简上言利害，见送三司相度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158495_comment'></div>况前后累经定夺，终无救之之效，以致为害益深，盖不能究其本原而急于近利使之然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158495_comment'></div>且茶课岁入数百万贯，所以助经费而宽调度，不可不审议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158495_comment'></div>欲望特降指挥，令三司将新旧之法，子细参详，定酌中之制，俾经久可行，委得公私利便，即具保明申奏，更乞朝廷再赐详酌施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158495_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论茶法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　皇祐四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158496")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158496'>臣访闻今岁江淮山场榷货务，见积压累年茶货一千一百馀万斤，并无客人算请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158496_comment'></div>盖自在京榷货务擘画，每茶引一百贯文，更贴纳三十四贯，方支得一百贯文茶货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158496_comment'></div>后来商旅阻节不行，每年课利并税钱亏欠数百万贯，则国家财用仰给何以取济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158496_comment'></div>今发运使施昌言近已到阙，欲乞令昌言与三司使副，将今来茶法子细公共从长定夺，合如何擘画，即得公私利济，经久可行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1158496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。十月，复三番使臣，拯极言其扰民之弊，请复罢之，不果。作品：请免接送北使三番。<div id='poem_1158485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请免接送北使三番奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158485")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158485'>臣近闻圣慈以接送契丹国人使往来，更不差三番，只令近上使臣管押金器，沿路充用，并委逐州县长吏通判及令佐已下，一切应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158485_comment'></div>中外闻之，莫不忻忭，以为数十年之弊，而陛下一旦罢去，使河北生灵有来苏之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158485_comment'></div>今闻内降指挥复置，臣未测缘由，徒用惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158485_comment'></div>且三番为河北之患，积有岁年，日甚一日，诛求搔扰，公私不胜其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158485_comment'></div>臣顷年曾差充送伴人使，且知蠹民残物之甚，亦尝论列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158485_comment'></div>缘河北连绵灾伤，流亡未复，若不省徭役，罢配率，以宽养凋瘵，是弃河朔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158485_comment'></div>况陛下矜念哀悯之极，故特行前诏，此为至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158485_comment'></div>今乃无故复置，窃为陛下痛惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158485_comment'></div>惟陛下特留圣意，且依前降指挥寝罢，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。因江浙、荆湖等路自去秋亢旱，米价甚高，民事不足。乞开义仓以济灾民。作品：请支义仓米赈给百姓。<div id='poem_1158477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请支义仓米赈给百姓奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（为监察御史时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158477")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158477'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158477'>臣访闻江浙、荆湖等路自去秋亢旱，田苗一例灾伤，即日米价甚高，民食不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158477_comment'></div>若不速令救济，必致流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158477_comment'></div>强壮者起为盗贼，老弱者转死沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158477_comment'></div>因此生事，为患不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158477_comment'></div>缘逐州除军粮常平仓外，别无大段斛斗准备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158477_comment'></div>窃知王琪见起请义仓，所在见管米数稍多，州县未必敢专辄支用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158477_comment'></div>若一一取候朝廷指挥，往复数月，当此艰食之际，恐无所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158477_comment'></div>欲望特降指挥，下逐路转运司勘会辖下元系灾伤州县，如委实人户阙食，即令画时将义仓米速行赈给，以济贫民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158477_comment'></div>如允臣所奏，即乞早赐指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158477_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。建言选用监察等官员，要精核治状，审验人才。作品：请选用提转长吏官。<div id='poem_1158387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选用提转长吏官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158387")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158387'>臣闻王者之总治天下也，内则宰臣、百执事，外则按察之官、刺史、县令而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158387_comment'></div>若中外各得其人，协心以济，则陛下垂拱仰成，无为无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158387_comment'></div>夫转运使、提点刑狱，在乎察官吏之能否，辨狱讼之冤滥，以至生民利病，财赋出入，莫不莅焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158387_comment'></div>事权至重，责任尤剧，设非其人，则一路受敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158387_comment'></div>如州县之职不举，按察之吏又不以闻，则朝廷无繇而知，是一方之民有终无告者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158387_comment'></div>昔汉宣帝曰：「与我共理天下者，其惟良二千石乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158387_comment'></div>盖刺史、县令，耳目接于民事，政令所出，惨舒攸系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158387_comment'></div>今朝廷既已轻授，又数数更易，其才者虽有育民济治之具，亦乌所施设哉，又况庸庸者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158387_comment'></div>今粗举一二，条陈如左：窃见近日除授转运使，但理资序，不甚选择，如江西路刘纬、利州路李熙辅，皆知识庸昧，众所共知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158387_comment'></div>其提点刑狱，亦未甚得人，若广西潘师旦、江东令狐挺、京西张士安、河东席平，皆素非干敏之才，又无廉洁之誉，猥当是选，宜乎不任其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158387_comment'></div>虽近例并委两制奏举，然所举之人，或才有合格，以微文不用，故不才者往往进焉，乃是诃其细而忽其大，恐非任才之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158387_comment'></div>欲乞今后应除转运使，先望实而后资考，则所得精矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158387_comment'></div>凡举提刑，若保荐之人不协公议，即乞责其谬举，别委他官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158387_comment'></div>如此，则可绝徇私之请矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158387_comment'></div>刺史、县令，前后条约，非不丁宁，其中滥进者亦众：如曹琰自通判便授润州大郡，果非理决人致死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158387_comment'></div>又闻韩松知鼎州，缘本州控接蛮界，居常屯治军马，旧系武臣知州，后乞选差文资，况韩松累任以不治闻，岂可当此边任乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158387_comment'></div>欲乞今后应差知州，并令有司精覈治状，审验人才，以州郡繁简要僻，差而授之，庶几不至败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158387_comment'></div>所有奏举县令，即令流内铨选注繁剧不治之邑，是则民瘼少苏，而和气可召矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158387_comment'></div>伏望圣慈申命宰府，举而行之，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1158387_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年3月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。弹宰相宋庠“窃位素餐”、无所建树，乞罢免之。作品：弹宋庠。<div id='poem_1158440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹宋庠奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐三年三月知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158440")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158440'>臣等今日中书传谕，奉圣旨宣示宋庠自辩及求退等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158440_comment'></div>臣等蒙陛下擢任，处之谏垣，惟采取天下公议，别白贤不肖，敷闻于上，冀陛下倚任常得其人，以熙大政，不使贪冒非才者得以胶固其位，害败于事，乃臣等之职分，陛下所责任者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158440_comment'></div>固不敢缘私诋欺，变白为黑，惑乱陛下耳目，动摇大臣爵位，以取奇誉，巧资身计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158440_comment'></div>斯亦臣等所自信，陛下所明照者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158440_comment'></div>臣等昨于二月二十二日，具劄子论列宋庠，自再秉衡轴，首尾七年，殊无建明，略效补报，而但阴拱持禄，窃位素餐，安处洋洋，以为得策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158440_comment'></div>且复求解之际，陛下降诏，未及断章，庠乃从容遂止其请，足见其固位无耻之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158440_comment'></div>今乃自辩，谓臣等议论暗合己意，臣等亦谓宋庠本意暗合天下之议论，斯不近于欺乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158440_comment'></div>陛下所深察矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158440_comment'></div>且云无过，则又不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158440_comment'></div>臣等窃以前代至于祖宗之朝，罢免执政大臣，莫不以其谟明无效，取群议而行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158440_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158440_comment'></div>执政大臣与国同体，不能尽心竭节，卓然树立，是谓之过，宜乎当黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158440_comment'></div>非如群有司小官之类，必有犯状挂于刑书，乃为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158440_comment'></div>唐宪宗朝，权德舆为宰相，不能有所发明，时人讥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158440_comment'></div>俄以循默而罢，复守本官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158440_comment'></div>宪宗，聪明仁爱之主也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158440_comment'></div>德舆，文学德行之臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158440_comment'></div>当时罢免，只缘循默，不必指瑕，未致罪名而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158440_comment'></div>至如祖宗朝，罢免范质、宋琪、李昉、张齐贤，亦只以不称职，均劳逸为辞，未尝明其过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158440_comment'></div>近岁方乃摭拾细故，托以为名，扬于外廷，斯乃不识大体之臣，上惑圣听，有乖举措，非所以责大臣之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158440_comment'></div>宋庠岂无细过，臣等不言之者，盖为陛下惜此事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158440_comment'></div>臣等所陈，惟陛下圣度详处，若以为是，则乞依前来劄子，早赐施行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158440_comment'></div>倘以臣等为谤讟时宰，敢肆狂妄，亦乞治正其罪，重行降黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158440_comment'></div>臣等无任激切俟命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1158440_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年4月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。建言由御史台督促该退之官员致仕，未果。作品：论百官致仕。<div id='poem_1158374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论百官致仕奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐三年四月知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158374")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158374'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158374'>伏以人臣之义，七十致仕，著在礼经，卓为明训，所以优假老成，遂其安逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158374_comment'></div>既不违达尊之教，且开知足之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158374_comment'></div>历代所钦，治宜敬切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158374_comment'></div>本朝典故，尤所重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158374_comment'></div>凡曰引年，莫非延世，推之半禄，待以优恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158374_comment'></div>其于惇劝之方，可谓至乎其至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158374_comment'></div>然而近岁寖成敝风，搢绅之閒，贪冒相尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158374_comment'></div>但顾子孙之计，殊愆羞恶之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158374_comment'></div>驰末景于桑榆，负厚颜于钟漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158374_comment'></div>不知其过，自以为得，诚非朝廷所以待士大夫之意，又非士大夫所以遵礼义之常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158374_comment'></div>臣思及此，悚然汗下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158374_comment'></div>伏望特降指挥御史台，将文武班簿检会，应臣僚年及七十，并令台牒讽其致仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158374_comment'></div>如牒举后三两日内，未见抗章祈请，乞自朝廷降令致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158374_comment'></div>所贵稍遏趋营之弊，颇惇廉耻之风。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158374_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年6月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。认为因着力于庆历新政而被贬斥的杨纮等人是无辜被遣，主张“复与甄擢”作品：请录用杨纮等。<span class='inlineComment2'>（不久，杨纮升任湖南转运使，王鼎提点河北路刑狱。）</span><div id='poem_1158400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请录用杨纮等奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158400")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158400'>臣读先朝实录，大中祥符中并、益二州岁满当代，先帝遍阅侍从官姓名，谓辅臣曰：「此等各有所长，然求其文雅适用，可委方面者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158400_comment'></div>每念有唐名贤，比肩而出，何当时得人之多也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158400_comment'></div>王旦等曰：「方今下位，岂无才俊，或恐拔擢未至尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158400_comment'></div>然观前代求贤，不求其备，不以小疵掩其大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158400_comment'></div>今兹立朝之士，谁为无过，陛下每务保庇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158400_comment'></div>然流言稍多，则亦梗于任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158400_comment'></div>大都迭相称誉近乎党，纠过讦非近乎公，鉴其爱憎，唯托上圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158400_comment'></div>诚哉是言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158400_comment'></div>至切至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158400_comment'></div>缘近世之患，正在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158400_comment'></div>以四海之广，不患无贤，而患在信用之不至尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158400_comment'></div>且顷岁以来，凡有才名之士，必遭险薄之辈假以他事中伤，殆乎屏弃，卒不得用，议者迄今痛惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158400_comment'></div>欲望圣慈申命宰执，应臣僚素有才行，先以非辜被谴，如杨纮、王鼎、王绰等，虽曾叙用，未复职任者，并乞复与甄擢，或委之繁剧，必有成效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158400_comment'></div>如是，则风化日益美，贤杰日益耸，积之以久，和气洽乎上下矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年7月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。新任知澶州李昭亮辞请它职，改授知成德军。拯上疏认为应严申命令，仍遣其澶州就任。作品：论李昭亮二章。<div id='poem_1158444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论李昭亮奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　皇祐三年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158444")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158444'>臣等伏见宣徽南院使、新知澶州李昭亮，因赴任到阙朝见，复有指挥，且令本院供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158444_comment'></div>虽天恩宽假，人欲必从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158444_comment'></div>然于事体有不可者，尤须为国家顾惜纲纪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158444_comment'></div>窃闻昭亮在延州日，尝累乞移近郡，而澶渊据北道之会，扼大河之津，朝廷素择重臣以镇之，是委遇之意不为不优矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158444_comment'></div>州境与畿甸相接，兼得以便私家之事，如昭亮所请，不为不从矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158444_comment'></div>以至增南院宣徽之重，诞告于廷而遣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158444_comment'></div>今始得觐，又欲遂留京师，前命废而不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158444_comment'></div>为昭亮计，诚可矣，恐非朝廷所以命大臣，而大臣于出处閒自持慎重之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158444_comment'></div>外议多云比来河流颇虞决溢之患，昭亮以此恳辞不去，又不可之尤甚者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158444_comment'></div>古所谓大臣者，能与天下国家同其休戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158444_comment'></div>今其名位兼中外之重，亦可以同休戚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158444_comment'></div>而计较一小利害，不肯宣力，矧天下利害固有大于此者，朝廷欲谁使哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158444_comment'></div>大臣举措果如此，将何以励小臣哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158444_comment'></div>伏望陛下依前降指挥，趣令赴任，上以全出命之体，下以存承命之信，无复开侥倖觊觎之路，由大臣始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158444_comment'></div>事体所系不细，臣等故敢极论之，惟望圣虑，必赐裁择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158444_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论李昭亮奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　皇祐三年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158445")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158445'>臣伏见宣徽南院使李昭亮近移知澶州，到阙朝见，遂乞留京师，复求边任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158445_comment'></div>臣等寻具论列，蒙指挥赐告三月，满日赴任，候边帅有阙，许令就移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158445_comment'></div>未逾数日，却除昭亮知真定府，移李昭述知秦州，替吕公绰赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158445_comment'></div>中外闻之，无不竦骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158445_comment'></div>且昭亮先在延州日，累求便郡，朝廷优进职名，特移近辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158445_comment'></div>既而又图边任，遽有此命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158445_comment'></div>是可否在于昭亮，而朝廷之命令不行，此岂大臣之所为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158445_comment'></div>兼昭述初授成德，公议已为不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158445_comment'></div>所莅之处，惟务姑息，在成德尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158445_comment'></div>缘秦州密接蕃部，最为巨屏，兵马素经训练，习知节制，乡来未尝轻授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158445_comment'></div>若一旦令昭述处之，遂用成德之政，必致士卒骄横，缓急决不可用，俾陕西沿边诸镇传闻，害事岂不大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158445_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降指挥，趣令昭亮依旧发赴澶州，昭述别与一郡，或且令在任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158445_comment'></div>公绰候将来满日，别选臣僚移替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158445_comment'></div>如此，则朝廷命令必行，不使侥倖觊觎之人得计，则纪纲自正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158445_comment'></div>事体所系不细，臣故敢再三极论之，必望圣虑裁择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1158445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年8月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。张尧佐再除宣徽南院使、判河阳。作品：弹张尧佐二章。<div id='poem_1158443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹张尧佐奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（三　皇祐二年闰十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158443")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158443'>臣伏见张尧佐除宣徽南院使、淮康军节度使，兼景灵宫使，又同群牧制置使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158443_comment'></div>制命一出，中外惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158443_comment'></div>缘张尧佐久以非才，滥司大计，利权反覆，物论沸腾，臣等累次论列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158443_comment'></div>陛下欲务保全，乃曲假宠荣，并领要职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158443_comment'></div>求之前代则无例，访以人情则不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158443_comment'></div>臣实忧危，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158443_comment'></div>窃惟陛下临御以来，凡所行事，悉遵守祖宗旧制，未尝踰越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158443_comment'></div>若乃进用臣僚，于先朝则李至、丁谓，自尚书参知政事授节度使，钱若水旧任枢密副使，由工部侍郎只得观察使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158443_comment'></div>于今朝则钱惟演以枢密使、兵部尚书授节度使，李士衡以三司使兼尚书右丞，李维以翰林学士承旨兼刑部尚书，陈尧咨以翰林学士兼工部侍郎，并授观察使，郑戬以资政殿大学士、户部侍郎知并州二年，只授宣徽使，踰年方加节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158443_comment'></div>此皆国朝之旧典也，自非德望兼著，亦不轻授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158443_comment'></div>今尧佐何者，而兼是四职乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158443_comment'></div>况执政大臣，与国休戚，不能执守建明，曲有阿徇，成此过举，俾天下窃议，谓陛下私于后宫，不独于圣德有损，抑又事体不可之至甚者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158443_comment'></div>伏望陛下以祖业为重，以天下为意，免使奸倖有所窥伺，特出宸断，罢尧佐宣徽使之命，任以外镇，庶可稍息天下之议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158443_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158534?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弹张尧佐奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　皇祐二年闰十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158534")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158534'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158534'>臣伏睹陛下即位仅三十年，奉承祖宗谟训，未有失道败德之事，陛下固知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158534_comment'></div>乃五六年来超擢张尧佐，群臣皆窃议于下，然而迹其过不在陛下，在女谒近习及执政大臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158534_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158534_comment'></div>盖女谒近习动伺陛下之所为，知陛下继嗣未立而有所私，莫不潜有趋向而附结之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158534_comment'></div>执政大臣不思规陛下以大义，乃从谀顺指，高官要职，惟恐尧佐不满其意，使陛下有私昵后宫之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158534_comment'></div>此岂爱君之心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158534_comment'></div>且以本朝故事言之：昭宪皇太后诞生祖宗，有基命之烈，其诸弟杜审肇辈穷老才有得一节度使者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158534_comment'></div>雷有终以工部侍郎讨平西川，得宣徽使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158534_comment'></div>李至于先朝有东宫之旧，自工部尚书参知政事，才用为武胜军节度使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158534_comment'></div>钱若水任枢密副使，李士衡以尚书左丞为三司使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158534_comment'></div>以及陛下之朝，李维为翰林学士承旨、刑部尚书，陈尧咨为翰林学士知开封府，并止换观察使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158534_comment'></div>夏竦立两府，自三司使户部尚书止得散节度使，后二年方加宣徽使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158534_comment'></div>郑戬亦曾任枢密副使，以资政殿大学士知并州，后方加宣徽使，又一年乃除节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158534_comment'></div>今尧佐谓之亲，则孰若杜审肇兄弟子？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158534_comment'></div>谓之贤，而功孰若雷有终、李至、钱若水乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158534_comment'></div>而宣徽、节度使并以与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158534_comment'></div>若非内外协应，蒙惑攘窃，宁至此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158534_comment'></div>尧佐叨据如此，惭羞不知，真清朝之秽污，白昼之魑魅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158534_comment'></div>况下制之日，阳精闇塞，氛雾继起，天道固于人事不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158534_comment'></div>伏望陛下断以大义，稍割爱情，追寝尧佐过越之恩，必不得已，宣徽、节度使择与其一，仍罢群牧制置使之命，俾之外部，以安全之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158534_comment'></div>如此，则仰合天意，俯顺人情，而重新盛德矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1158534_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年9月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。皇祐三年九月十一日，诏令拯与三司河渠司等同议塞商胡、郭固决河。作品：论修商胡口。<div id='poem_1158486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论修商胡口奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158486")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158486'>臣伏睹近降敕命，商胡口只候来年秋修塞，合要物料，令三司检会天禧年修河体例敷配，所贵众力易集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158486_comment'></div>臣先奉圣旨，与两制以上定夺修闭利害，以商胡经久，须合修塞，方免河北水患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158486_comment'></div>今准指挥，来秋修塞，必是河水令归故道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158486_comment'></div>缘前来累经差官相度工役五十馀万，三二年閒恐未了毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158486_comment'></div>若河水𣿬注，未得通快，则商胡固难豫修，修之则溃溢之害立可待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158486_comment'></div>况顷岁之决，祇以故道横陇壅阏，水势不快，遂致溃溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158486_comment'></div>今若不先议开理水道，使之浚流，便欲修塞商胡，不惟必有后患，乃是重起八年科率之弊，虚困六路凋残之民耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158486_comment'></div>欲乞朝廷且据计度到故道工役，先令差拨兵夫，渐次开理，或一二年内，功可必就，即委三司豫行计置物料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158486_comment'></div>若是全出民閒，事必难集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158486_comment'></div>盖诸路久经灾伤，虽京东、京西、河北、陕西近岁稍稔，然富者竭于率敛，贫者见已流离，倘不恤他虞，遽兴大役，臣恐朝廷之忧不独在商胡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158486_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特出宸断，以河朔久罹水患，须议疏塞，即乞且辍那内藏库见钱百万贯，令三司专功收管，积薪聚粮，豫为具备，其馀即令中等已上人户敷配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158486_comment'></div>候开淘旧道，水有所归，则商胡之塞，一举可成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158486_comment'></div>所贵民力稍宽，功用无乏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158486_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年秋</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。荐范祥任陕西转运副使。作品：再举范祥。<div id='poem_1158399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再举范祥奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158399")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158399'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158399'>臣先自陕西相度盐法回，曾具劄子，乞除提点刑狱范祥权本路转运副使，所贵擘画盐法利害，计置沿边斛斗，事归一局，易为办集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158399_comment'></div>至今未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158399_comment'></div>勘会范祥新法，自皇祐元年正月至二年十二月终，共收到见钱二百八十九万一千贯有零，比较旧法，二年计增钱五十一万六千贯有零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158399_comment'></div>三年春季又已收到见钱七十馀万贯，兼籴到斛斗万数不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158399_comment'></div>缘陕西累岁丰熟，今秋又大稔，正当计置之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158399_comment'></div>况范祥显著成效，可备驱策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158399_comment'></div>欲望圣慈允臣前奏，特许就除范祥本路转运副使，责其久任，俾之一面制置解盐，及将见钱收籴粮斛，须管沿边军储，大段有备，又免向去入中枉费榷货务见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158399_comment'></div>经久之利，无便于此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1158399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年10月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。谓淑不尽侍养之责，妄驰仕进，请罢其职。作品：弹李淑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。仁宗皇祐三年十月，吴奎知密州。拯奏乞留奎。作品：请留吴奎依旧供职。<div id='poem_1158465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请留吴奎依旧供职奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158465")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158465'>臣伏闻敕差起居舍人吴奎知密州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158465_comment'></div>臣近因上殿，亲奉德音宣谕，以唐介弹奏大臣，事及吴奎，臣亦粗陈本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158465_comment'></div>缘吴奎荷陛下不次擢用，孜孜言事，不避权倖，以是忌嫉者众，非陛下英明博照，无保全之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158465_comment'></div>况唐介轻妄之词，诬罔天听，固圣鉴悉以辨明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158465_comment'></div>臣以无状，待罪谏列，不能补报，以负天下之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158465_comment'></div>岂可见朝廷事有过举，循默不言，而令谏官横被恶名哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158465_comment'></div>虽吴奎补郡，私愿甚便，然公议痛惜之，伏望圣慈且令依旧供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158465_comment'></div>臣区区之心，非为吴奎，所惜者朝廷事体，盖不欲使奸邪者得计，则臣之责塞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158465_comment'></div>惟圣度曲赐裁察，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158465_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年11月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。江淮六路连岁亢旱，民食艰阻，流亡者多。拯上疏请免江淮六路灾伤州县之配籴及诸般科率。作品：请救济江淮饥民。<div id='poem_1158476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请救济江淮饥民奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158476")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158476'>臣闻天以五星为府，人以五谷为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158476_comment'></div>五星紊于上，则灾异起于下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158476_comment'></div>九谷绝于野，则盗贼兴于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158476_comment'></div>天之于人，上下相应，故天变于其上，则人乱于其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158476_comment'></div>是天人相与之际，甚可畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158476_comment'></div>若变异上著，则恐惧修省，以谢于下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158476_comment'></div>年谷不登，则赈贷予赉，而恤其困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158476_comment'></div>盖不使天有大变，而民有饥色，则人获富寿，而国享安宁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158476_comment'></div>方今灾异之变尤甚，臣近已论列详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158476_comment'></div>惟江淮六路连岁亢旱，民食艰阻，流亡者比比皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158476_comment'></div>朝廷昨遣使命安抚赈贷，以救其敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158476_comment'></div>而东南岁运上供米六百万石，近虽减一百万石，缘逐路租税尽已蠲复，则粮斛从何而出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158476_comment'></div>未免州县配粜，以充其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158476_comment'></div>由是民閒所出，悉输入官，民储已竭，配者未已，纵有米价，率无可粜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158476_comment'></div>父子皇皇，相顾不救，老弱者死于沟洫，少壮者聚为盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158476_comment'></div>不幸奸雄乘閒而起，则不可制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158476_comment'></div>当以何道而卒安之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158476_comment'></div>且国家之患，未有不缘此而致，可不熟虑乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158476_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降指挥，应江淮六路灾伤州县，凡是配粜及诸般科率，一切止绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158476_comment'></div>如敢故犯，并坐违制，庶几少释疲民倒垂之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158476_comment'></div>其上供米数，若不敷元额，即候向去丰熟补填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158476_comment'></div>仍令州县官吏，多方擘画，救济饥民，不得失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158476_comment'></div>兼委逐路提、转专切提举，如不用心救济，以致流亡，及结成群党，即乞一例重行降黜。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1158476'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1158476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年冬</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。殿中侍御史里行唐介力弹劾宰相文彦博“阴结贵妃”“显用尧佐”，包拯、吴奎与之相连。唐、吴被贬，拯亦求外任，未果。作品：求外任七章。<div id='poem_1158526' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158526' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158526?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求外任奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一　皇祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158526")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158526_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158526'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158526'>臣以极陋至庸之质，过叨甄擢，猥参近侍，仍预谏职，才微负重，何以云补！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158526_comment'></div>伏惟陛下以英睿之德，兼夷旷之度，询求谠议，容纳愚直，此诚臣百千载之一遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158526_comment'></div>然以位疏言贱，罕或施行，上则负陛下求治之心，下则忤执政用才之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158526_comment'></div>且忠良介特之士在下既不能进，奸猾苛暴之人居职又不能退，公议日迫，无以逃责，久兹忝冒，实不皇宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158526_comment'></div>伏望陛下悯以无他，矜乎不逮，宽其罪戾，赐以保全，俾出领于单麾，庶少图于薄效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158526_comment'></div>臣欲乞江浙一次知州任使，臣无任恳愿激切之至<span class='inlineComment2'>（《包拯集》卷一○。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158526_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1158526'>皇祐三年：原无，下六篇同，按此以下七奏皆包拯乞罢知谏院补外任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158526_comment'></div>其末篇在皇祐三年冬<span class='inlineComment2'>（见该篇校记）</span>，则馀六篇亦当在此前不久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158526_comment'></div>拯以二年春始知谏院，故奏中言「到院未及二年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158526_comment'></div>至四年三月仁宗乃从其请，出为河北都转运使。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158526_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求外任奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　皇祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158527")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158527'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158527'>臣近者上殿，曾具劄子进呈，乞江浙一次知州任使，至今未奉指挥，进退悚惧，启处不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158527_comment'></div>窃念臣识闇材驽，任优责重，于国家之大事无可济，于朝廷之庶务不能周，献替既无所闻，论议又不足信，冒荣滋久，腼颜不皇，退揣至庸，愿全素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158527_comment'></div>伏望陛下曲回圣造，俯谅愚衷，特与保全，俾从外任，誓图报效，靡惮捐縻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158527_comment'></div>臣无任祈恩俟命激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1158527_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158528' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158528' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求外任奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（三　皇祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158528")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158528'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158528'>臣生于草茅，蚤从宦学，尽信前书之载，窃慕古人之为，知事君行己之方，有竭忠死义之分，确然素守，期以勉循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158528_comment'></div>而况亲逢盛辰，骤被殊用，寘诸侍从之列，擢处谏诤之班，臣于此时敢忘图报！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158528_comment'></div>至于朝廷之政或阙，国家之计所先，爵宠非贤，权倖干进，臣尝披沥肝胆，冒犯威颜，是忌讳之不知，曷怨仇之足避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158528_comment'></div>滥当所职，既竭乃心，然才无所长，愚有不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158528_comment'></div>虽閒形于狂瞽，徒仰紊于睿聪，止成塞责之虚名，讵见已行之实效！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158528_comment'></div>犬马之贱，岂惮沟壑之弃捐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158528_comment'></div>尘露之微，无裨山海之高大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158528_comment'></div>上则孤圣君之盛选，下乃迫多士之公言，势难茍安，理宜知退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158528_comment'></div>向者屡陈封削，未赐允俞，尚出入于轩闱，每惭羞于面目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158528_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下察臣愚直，匪为身谋，悯臣孱微，所忧任重，从其危恳，委以外藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158528_comment'></div>献替之司，庶免妨贤之咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158528_comment'></div>循良之寄，誓坚尽瘁之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158528_comment'></div>干触冕旒，臣无任祈恩俟命恳迫激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1158528_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求外任奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（四　皇祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158529")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158529_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158529'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158529'>臣近曾陈乞外任差遣，蒙降中书劄子，奉圣旨令依旧供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158529_comment'></div>伏念臣立朝孤直，荷圣奖知，每竭肺肝，勉图报塞，虽夙夜匪懈，务进瞽言，而岁月逾深，讫无善状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158529_comment'></div>臣当坚辞所职，退避能贤，思之甚详，志方不夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158529_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下察臣危迫，惠此顽冥，特霈俞音，俾分便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158529_comment'></div>茍全要领，幸出于回容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158529_comment'></div>誓竭糜捐，终酬于覆载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158529_comment'></div>臣无任祈恩俟命激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1158529_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求外任奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（五　皇祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158530")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158530'>臣近者累次陈乞外任差遣，蒙降中书劄子，奉圣旨令依旧供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158530_comment'></div>寻再具状陈乞，未蒙指挥施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158530_comment'></div>伏念臣夙以愚直，无所云补，久污高明之地，弥负素餐之责，愿避贤路，庶塞公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158530_comment'></div>伏望陛下矜其拙讷，赐以保全，俾领郡麾，少图涓效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158530_comment'></div>臣无任恳悃俟命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158530_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158531?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求外任奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（六　皇祐三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158531")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158531_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158531'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158531'>臣前后六次具状并劄子陈乞外任差遣，近又准中书劄子，奉圣旨以臣到院未及二年，依天禧元年新降诏书，令依旧供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158531_comment'></div>臣迹孤望轻，才短责重，上不能广圣主之德，下不及救当时之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158531_comment'></div>若乃不愧屋漏，罔恤人言，虽茍逭于邦刑，恐难逃于阴谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158531_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下察其审分，鉴此由衷，特推从欲之恩，免罹非据之咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158531_comment'></div>冒渎宸听，臣无任激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158531_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158532?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求外任奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（七　皇祐三年冬）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158532")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158532'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158532'>臣近以起居舍人吴奎差知密州，曾具论列，未赐施行，进退忧惶，罔知攸措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158532_comment'></div>伏念臣孤危之迹，多仇少与，待罪谏列，垂及二年，竟不能有所建明，少裨万一，而陛下圣度渊深，终赐保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158532_comment'></div>虽明主之恩不忍轻去，在愚臣之分固难自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158532_comment'></div>伏望圣慈指挥，检会臣前后累次陈乞外任差遣因依，许除江浙一便郡，誓殚薄效，上答鸿恩，臣无任恳迫俟命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1158532_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。发运使许元绩用颇著，当别有进擢。乞依许元例，另置发运判官一名。作品：请置发运判官。<div id='poem_1158393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158393?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请置发运判官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐二年十一月知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158393")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158393_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158393'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158393'>臣窃以京师众大之都，屯兵数十万，财用储廪，皆仰给于东南，主是任者，制置发运使最为今之剧职，固不可轻以授人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158393_comment'></div>况朝廷参用两制，假以事权，委付之重，不谓不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158393_comment'></div>伏见发运使许元，先自判官，凡莅职八年，东南利害，无不周悉，所以岁运不乏者，盖久任得人之明效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158393_comment'></div>缘施昌言、许元绩用颇著，窃虑别有进擢，则后来虽有才者，必恐未能究财用出入之敝，则无繇办集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158393_comment'></div>臣欲乞依许元例，令置判官一员，于朝臣内选差素有公望干才者充，如前久任，所贵稔熟其事，嗣守成规，或昌言等缓急替移，免致败事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158393_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。知虔州余靖丁忧。作品：请选人知虔州。<div id='poem_1158401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选人知虔州奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158401")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158401'>臣伏见虔州据江表上游，南控岭徼，兵民财赋，素号重地，累岁盗贼充斥，如类行者，结集群党，大为民害，近方稍息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158401_comment'></div>今闻南雄猺贼唐才旺等，所至惊劫，杀害官吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158401_comment'></div>况封境与本州接连，最是控扼之所，全藉才干长吏与之绥辑备御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158401_comment'></div>昨朝廷特差余靖，近又丁忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158401_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特降指挥，令审官院选差有方略强明臣僚，往彼知州，庶一方之民得获便安。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158401_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。旧开矾铺进纳授官人李授男与故申王宫承俊为亲，拯乞罢其婚媾。作品：论李绶冒国亲事。<div id='poem_1158461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论李绶冒国亲事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐四年知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158461")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158461'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158461'>臣窃闻旧开矾铺进纳授官人李绶男与故申王宫承俊为亲，将就婚卺，中外传闻，莫不骇愕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158461_comment'></div>检会御史台编敕节文，应皇属议亲，并令具门阀次第，委宗正寺官审覆，须的是衣冠之后，非阘冗庸贱之伍，富商大贾之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158461_comment'></div>差涉不实，会赦不原其罪，仍仰抨弹之官常加采听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158461_comment'></div>又太常礼院敕大宗正司奏，不是工商伎术之家，听许为亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158461_comment'></div>其李绶男正碍条制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158461_comment'></div>窃以伉合之序，贵于匹敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158461_comment'></div>氏族之选，属在名胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158461_comment'></div>盖礼教之重，所宜谨严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158461_comment'></div>人地之华，必资参择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158461_comment'></div>按李绶阘茸之馀，轩裳所绝，向缘进纳，已滥宠恩，岂可更冒渎国姻，尘鄙公族，使天支之秀，下偶非类，汩紊彝制，亏损朝美？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158461_comment'></div>臣请罢其婚媾，别求德阀，仍乞申命有司，今后国亲并须依敕选定。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158461_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。认为魏征之谏言亦可行于今日，故录其三疏上于仁宗，请置天子座右。作品：进魏郑公三疏札子。<div id='poem_1158361' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158361' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158361?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进魏郑公三疏劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（为天章阁待制知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158361")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158361_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158361'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158361'>臣闻唐太宗英明好谏之主也，魏玄成忠直无隐之臣也，故君臣道合，千载一时，事无不言，言无不纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158361_comment'></div>太宗尝谓左右曰：「朕即位之初，或言人主必须威权独运，不得委任群下，或欲耀兵振武，慑服四夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158361_comment'></div>惟有玄成劝朕偃革兴文，布德施惠，中国既安，远人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1158361", 1158361, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>自服</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158361_comment'></div>朕从其语，天下大宁，绝域君长，皆来朝贡，此皆玄成之力也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158361_comment'></div>是故贞观之风与三代比盛，垂三百年，抑有繇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158361_comment'></div>所上谏疏，具在史册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158361_comment'></div>臣窃谓玄成虽言于当日，亦可行于方今，谨条其三疏，备录于左，皆词理切直，可为龟鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158361_comment'></div>伏望陛下万几之暇，特赐观览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158361_comment'></div>傅说曰：「知之非艰，行之惟艰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158361_comment'></div>惟陛下少留圣意，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1158361_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。上仁宗要务七事，皆当时之要务，希望仁宗留神省察。<div id='poem_1158362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158362?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上仁宗要务七事奏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158362")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158362_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1158362_0'>① 皇祐三年上，时为天章阁待制知谏院</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158362'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158362'>臣非材备位谏职，思所以为补报者，惟言责而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158362_comment'></div>然言不激切，则不足开宸虑而补圣政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158362_comment'></div>谨条上七事，皆当今之要务，词理鄙直，惟陛下留神省察：一事：臣伏以陛下天纵宽仁，海纳谋议，是者取而施用，非者存而掩覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158362_comment'></div>群下见圣度闳博，不以是非，皆能容受，故奸邪敢肆矫妄，持难明不然之事，巧饰厚诬，使人无由自辩，而默受排斥之祸，至陛下明有所蔽，疑贰忠良，率以此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158362_comment'></div>夫忠良见疑，则忠义之臣欲竭节尽忠补报陛下者，皆惧谗畏祸，不敢挺然当国家之事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158362_comment'></div>由是阴奸得计，滋长弊病，不惟有亏圣德，致害时政，一旦缓急，乏才贤以使，陛下持大任，将谁付之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158362_comment'></div>臣愿陛下听纳群下谋议之际，留神深察，如有持难明不然之事，巧饰厚诬于人者，请付有司责其明辩，使真伪不杂，是非较然，则忠邪自分，天下庶几于理矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158362_comment'></div>二事：臣伏闻近岁以来，多有指名臣下为朋党者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158362_comment'></div>其閒奋不顾身，孜孜于国，奖善嫉恶，激浊扬清之人，尤被奸巧诬罔，例见排斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158362_comment'></div>故进一贤士，必曰朋党相助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158362_comment'></div>退一庸才，亦曰朋党相嫉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158362_comment'></div>遂使正人结舌，忠直息心，不敢公言是非，明示劝诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158362_comment'></div>此最为国之大患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158362_comment'></div>夫圣明在上，未尝闻有朋党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158362_comment'></div>朋党之来，大抵起于衰闇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158362_comment'></div>故汉之党锢始安帝，而极于桓、灵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158362_comment'></div>唐之朋党由穆宗，而甚于文、武：是皆衰闇之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158362_comment'></div>以陛下用心图治，功同尧、舜，讵可如汉、唐衰闇之际，而致有朋党乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1158362_comment'></div>斯乃臣下务相倾轧，自快其志，加诸其人，不顾破坏陛下事业者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1158362_comment'></div>在昔刘向进谏于汉元帝曰：「孔子与颜渊、子贡更相称誉，不为朋党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1158362_comment'></div>禹、稷与皋陶转相汲引，不为比周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1158362_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1158362_comment'></div>忠于为国，无邪心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1158362_comment'></div>又曰：「贤人在上位，则引其类而聚之于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1158362_comment'></div>在下位，则思与其类俱进」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1158362_comment'></div>臣谓刘向之言，垂千馀年，谈者以为至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1158362_comment'></div>臣诚学向者也，不忍以熙洽之朝有朋党之说，亏损至德，蔽塞大明，臣实痛伤不能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1158362_comment'></div>臣愿陛下端虑以临下，推诚以格物，循名以核其实，因迹以照其心，使忠者、邪者情伪毕见，勿以朋党为意，则君子、小人区以别矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1158362_comment'></div>三事：臣伏闻顷岁大臣颛政，颇恶才能之士，有所开建，则讥其近名，或云沽激，欲求进达，遂使才能之士莫敢自效，纵能不顾忌讳，指陈事理，固亦困于沮挠，无得而施用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1158362_comment'></div>且名者，圣贤之所贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1158362_comment'></div>孔子曰：「君子疾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1158362", 1158362, "Clauses/124/Comments/2")'>没世</span>而名不称焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1158362_comment'></div>贾子曰：「烈士徇名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1158362_comment'></div>人不顾名，何以趋善？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1158362_comment'></div>圣人所以贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1158362_comment'></div>夫群下虽众，然士有志于国家之急者甚少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1158362_comment'></div>其能处心积虑图报于上，又困于近名之说，是则志士仁人终无以奖进矣，岂陛下之心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1158362_comment'></div>此诚顷岁大臣之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1158362_comment'></div>臣愿陛下但顾其所臧否而亟行之，勿以近名沽激求进为念，则人得以尽其心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1158362_comment'></div>四事：臣闻议者云：陛下颇主先入之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1158362_comment'></div>臣以陛下通照于事，务得情伪，理必无之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1158362_comment'></div>万一或有，臣止可过虑而议，不可闻之而不言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1158362_comment'></div>臣谓帝王行事，但顾理道之如何尔，固不计于先入后陈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1158362_comment'></div>必若主先入者以为是邪，则奸罔之人逞其敏捷，或巧中人，或阴图事，惟恐居其后矣，得不惑乱于耳目哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1158362_comment'></div>臣愿陛下采纳群议之际，但顾其事之是非，裁之以当，则先入之患息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1158362_comment'></div>五事：臣伏见近日以来，科禁多有疑下之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1158362_comment'></div>如举御史，须荐二员，上自点定，仍有在京与外任之拘，及见任二府曾举奏之人，亦不详论，至与中书、枢密院，止许旬假见客，及不许百官巡厅，台谏官不得私谒，并与刑法官接见雪罪叙劳之人等事，皆非帝王推诚尽下之美政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1158362_comment'></div>以陛下至德难名，待物无閒，方将拟迹尧、舜，固非汉武雄猜多忌之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1158362_comment'></div>斯盖不识大体之臣，过防谬论，上误陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1158362_comment'></div>臣恐书之史册，取讥万古，愿陛下速革近制，推大信于群下，以景祐初年之政为法，则尽美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1158362_comment'></div>六事：臣伏见近岁以来，灾异备至，天象谪见，地理倾震，虫蝗为孽，水旱作沴，连绵三数年未已，而河北最甚，其次利州、京东西、两浙、河东路，循环皆被大患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1158362_comment'></div>以陛下焦劳求理，恐一物失其所，持此寅畏，宁不感召和气，格上天之福禄乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1158362_comment'></div>然而致如此者，盖大臣不能同寅协恭，知无不为，切救时弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1158362_comment'></div>而陛下志虑亦或有疑沮，未能委任忠贤，以成垂拱之美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1158362_comment'></div>方今诸路饥馑，万姓流离，府库空虚，财力匮乏，官有数倍之滥，廪无二年之蓄，兵卒骄惰，夷狄盛强，即不幸继以凶年，加之小寇，则何人可以倚仗而枝梧哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1158362_comment'></div>臣所以夙夜怵惕，思进苦言，冀开悟陛下而不能已已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1158362_comment'></div>臣愿陛下切留宸虑，密以事诏今之执政，谁能尽心敢救天下之弊，敢当天下之责者，果得其人，愿陛下主张而委任之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1158362_comment'></div>其阴拱循默，持禄取容，妒嫉贤能，以一己为计者，宜速罢免，毋俾久塞要路，则化危为安，变艰于易，如反掌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1158362_comment'></div>陛下固不可失此时而不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1158362_comment'></div>傥失此时而不为，祸变一发，则虽欲为而不可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1158362_comment'></div>惟陛下深存念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1158362_comment'></div>七事：臣伏见近岁以来，多有窜逐之臣，或以无罪，或因小过，或为阴邪排陷，或由权要憎嫉，吹毛求其疵点，洗垢出其瘢痕，罪罟实繁，刑网太密，甚伤清议，大郁舆情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1158362_comment'></div>昔匹妇含怨，三年亢阳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1158362_comment'></div>匹夫怀愤，六月飞霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1158362_comment'></div>近岁窜逐之人，讵止匹夫匹妇之伦也，得不逆和气召灾沴乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1158362_comment'></div>陛下固宜矜体而深惟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1158362_comment'></div>传曰：「使功不如使过」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1158362_comment'></div>盖负责之人，自忿废绝，不能振起；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1158362_comment'></div>一旦为明主弃瑕录用，则其自奋图报，倍万常人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1158362_comment'></div>愿陛下诏近岁窜逐之臣，有才行效实，而本无过累，洎坐累获罪之轻者，或加牵复，或加宠擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1158362_comment'></div>如此，则圣造洪覆，同天之仁，使排陷憎嫉之风不敢复为矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1158362_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。言仁宗当善于用人。作品：论委任大臣。<div id='poem_1158363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论委任大臣奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158363")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158363'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158363'>臣尝读《汉书·谷永传》曰：「帝王之德莫大于知人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158363_comment'></div>诚哉，是言也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158363_comment'></div>夫王者端居岩廊之上，垂拱而仰成者，以能知人，能官人，使之然尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158363_comment'></div>或异于是，则虽尧、舜之焦劳癯瘠，亦不能成无为之化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158363_comment'></div>伏惟陛下以明睿之姿，励精求治之切，中外臣僚，才与不才，固无有能逃圣鉴者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158363_comment'></div>且丞弼之重，最为今之极选，而治乱系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158363_comment'></div>若乃挺然尽心，敢任天下之责者，即当委而付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158363_comment'></div>设或拱默取容，以徇一身之利者，亦当罢而去之，惟在陛下神机洞照，甄别而信任之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158363_comment'></div>若任而不择，择而不精，非止不能为治，抑所以为害矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158363_comment'></div>夫近臣中素有公望实才，众所谓贤者，陛下既得而知之，亦宜亟擢而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158363_comment'></div>若知而不能用，用而不能尽其才，何以致理哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158363_comment'></div>不可以边陲不耸，恬然便谓无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158363_comment'></div>况诸路饥馑相继，财用不足，府库虚竭，士卒骄惰，振举纪律，杜绝萌渐，正是可为之时，固宜参用贤者，助成治体，此尤不可缓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158363_comment'></div>大抵今之居位者，挟奸佞则蔽善而背公，溺爱憎则卖直而嫁祸，𧬈𧬈然但以势利相轧，茍得无耻，岂有援贤进能之意乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1158363_comment'></div>傥令如是辈比肩并进，而望风俗日益美，教化日益成，其可得哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1158363_comment'></div>论者皆曰：今若以廉直退让有才之士，择焉而用，置诸左右，则向日之失立可矫正，而邪谄茍且忌刻奸险之徒当不令而去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1158363_comment'></div>陛下何惮而不为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1158363_comment'></div>臣以孤贱之徒，叨居言责之任，图所以为报者，惟思倾竭愚虑，庶可上裨圣政万分之一，愿陛下少留神明，则天下蒙幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1158363_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。建言由武将充任河北等第官员，责守备抚驭之术。作品：请选河北知州。<div id='poem_1158389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选河北知州奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158389")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158389'>臣送伴北使往回，窃见河北当路州军，各系近边控扼之地，所有知州等，并是朝廷一一精选，盖欲谨边防，训士卒，以为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158389_comment'></div>今则不然，但能增饰厨传，迎送使人，及曲奉过客，便为称职，则美誉日闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158389_comment'></div>若稍异于此，则谤议纷然，往往因此降黜者有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158389_comment'></div>缘每年两次人使往来，动经七八个月，逐处豫为准备，不敢少懈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158389_comment'></div>况去岁两度非次人使，乃是一年之内迎送绝无虚日，又何暇略谋训练哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158389_comment'></div>兼访闻北虏日夕点集兵马，添创营寨，但以西讨为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158389_comment'></div>然戎狄之心殊不可测，议者虽云盟誓坚固，万无负德，且安不忘危，利或生害，又况已然之兆，不可不预为之备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158389_comment'></div>臣观一路武臣，未甚得人，但售进市恩，结挟弭谤尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158389_comment'></div>一旦急用，必无成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158389_comment'></div>加以边备未完，边廪未实，茍有骚动，将何取济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158389_comment'></div>此朝廷所宜深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158389_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后应缘边及当路知州部署钤辖驻泊等，并武臣中，不以官位高下，但选擢有武艺将材可用者任之，专责以守备抚驭之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158389_comment'></div>如有实效，不可以浮议数有移替，俾军民安其政令，缓急不至败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158389_comment'></div>如允臣所奏，即乞特赐指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。言河北事体至大，连岁水旱，帅臣长吏尤在的人。作品：论河北帅臣二章。<div id='poem_1158396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论河北帅臣奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158396")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158396'>臣伏见河北自商胡决溢之后，连岁水旱，仓廪匮乏，调度不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158396_comment'></div>朝廷一切应副，广有馀年之蓄，而流亡未尽复，田亩未尽辟，诸州长吏尤在得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158396_comment'></div>其閒茍且之辈，但干寻常事务，趋过目前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158396_comment'></div>其经久利害，知不及其身，率皆不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158396_comment'></div>前后相承，积弊已极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158396_comment'></div>至帅臣亦未甚精选，或有不乐久任者，乞后阙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1158396_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1158397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论河北帅臣奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158397")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158397'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158397'>臣伏见河北自商胡决溢之后，连岁水旱，仓廪匮乏，可不深思远虑而忽天戒也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158397_comment'></div>臣近上言，以河朔连岁灾伤，公私匮乏，帅臣长吏尤在得人，其有不愿久任者，乞于中外臣僚中，推择谙知彼中事宜，敢任大责者，专委付之，俾绥抚疲民，经画远图，庶几后患可弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158397_comment'></div>且河朔之于京畿，犹心腹之与背膂，义同一体，休戚均之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158397_comment'></div>今灾异如是，岂可坐视其敝，恬然以为无事，但欲因循，惮于更张措置可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158397_comment'></div>臣实惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158397_comment'></div>惟陛下留神省察，以河北事体至大，帅臣等可用可罢，速赐神断，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1158397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。请既要发挥谏官的作用，又要严防其营私舞弊。作品：论台官言事。<div id='poem_1158373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论台官言事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（为天章阁待制知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158373")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158373_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158373'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158373'>臣伏见近者台官以朝政阙失，上章论列，或令分析，或取戒励，中外传闻，于体不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158373_comment'></div>且国家置御史府者，盖防臣僚不法，时政失宜，朝廷用之为纪纲，人君委之如耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158373_comment'></div>所以先帝特降诏书，添置侍御史以下六员，并不兼领职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158373_comment'></div>当时诏令不允官曹涉私，措置乖方，刑赏踰制，并许弹奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158373_comment'></div>虽言有过当，必示曲全；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158373_comment'></div>若事难显行，即令留内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158373_comment'></div>盖先帝切于求治，如是之极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158373_comment'></div>伏自陛下临御以来，将三十载，遵守先训，广开言路，虚怀以待，犯颜必容，此皆陛下忧勤庶政之至深，群臣仰望清光之不暇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158373_comment'></div>臣欲望今后御史等凡有弹奏，事或过当，更不令分析及取戒励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158373_comment'></div>若乃阿意徇私，即乞重行责降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158373_comment'></div>如此，则上彰陛下好谏之德，下免朝廷过举之失。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1158373_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。举荐韩贽、孙抗、阎询等人重回御史台。作品：请复韩贽等台官。<div id='poem_1158395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请复韩贽等台官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158395")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158395'>臣窃见祠部员外郎韩贽、屯田员外郎孙抗、太常博士阎询等，才识明茂，资质纯正，先任御史，各以微累黜免，多历年所，屡经恩宥，勘会前来，所坐原情，且非大故，弃瑕亦合录用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158395_comment'></div>况御史台阙官甚众，奏举罕得其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158395_comment'></div>如贽等，求之方今，实为精选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158395_comment'></div>臣以谓可复旧职，必允清议，伏望圣慈特召还台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158395_comment'></div>或不如所举，臣甘当同罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。阎士良由六宅副使除授崇仪使，拯上疏乞移其别路差遣。作品：论阎士良转官。<div id='poem_1158463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论阎士良转官奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158463")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158463'>臣等伏见六宅副使阎士良除授崇仪使，罔测缘繇，中外疑惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158463_comment'></div>盖自明堂覃恩之后，臣僚非著灼然功效，未尝有超越迁转者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158463_comment'></div>按士良先任蔡州都监日，以不法坐罪，黜降不逾数年，复升职任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158463_comment'></div>今又不次骤正使名，物议喧然，以为不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158463_comment'></div>且河朔塘水当无事之时，亦可助边防之固，但存旧制，公私为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158463_comment'></div>顷岁杨怀敏兴修不已，大为民患，累有臣僚论列，遂令依旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158463_comment'></div>自士良继领是职，访闻复以创置屯田为名，疏决水势，飘浸乡村，沿塞居民，尤被其苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158463_comment'></div>况逐州军自属长吏等筦构，岂假更设斯局！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158463_comment'></div>兼士良到阙奏事，仅及两月，迁延不去，必是以此为功，邀求进秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158463_comment'></div>既得之后，何所不至！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158463_comment'></div>寖开侥倖之路，或构戎虏之隙，则为害不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158463_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特许追夺前命，以戒将来，及移士良与别路差遣，庶免向去别启衅端。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1158463_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。长子繶娶淮阳崔氏女。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年2月</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。言利州一路累经灾伤，而转运使李熙辅不才庸谬，难当重任。乞另选廉敏才识之士，充利州路转运。作品：请选利州路转运使。<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐四年二月三日，降利州路转运使、度支郎中李熙辅知商州。）</span><div id='poem_1158391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请选利州路转运使奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐四年初知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158391")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158391'>臣伏见中书劄子，知巴州杨佐奏：「昨体量得巡检顿士宁为事过当，非理打骂兵士，州司取勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158391_comment'></div>及提刑、转运使巡历到州，问顿士宁有何不协，只一向盘问所劾官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158391_comment'></div>况顿士宁与李熙辅有旧恩，作本司采访施行，若顿士宁指论臣，诏法何以遵守」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158391_comment'></div>又见本路提刑司奏：「巴州见禁巡检顿士宁并兵士等，及转运使李熙辅到彼审问，据顿士宁口称屈抑，及分析知州不公事，一面行遣差官往彼推勘，及差利州通判史世隆往巴州权交替知州，杨佐赴置院照勘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158391_comment'></div>奉圣旨：「令提刑司选清强官，依公尽理，取勘施行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158391_comment'></div>窃缘杨佐见为长吏，部下官属既有不公，理合体量按问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158391_comment'></div>今李熙辅乃凭信顿士宁分析，一面差官往彼交替，杨佐赴置院照勘，显是熙辅与士宁有旧，挟私任性，不遵诏敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158391_comment'></div>若令举劾之，妄被诬构，便下所司与人对勘，则今后部下官属有过，长吏顾避不敢按问，乃是废格诏敕，而容长奸恶，此尤事体不可之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158391_comment'></div>兼熙辅不才庸谬，众所共知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1158391_comment'></div>臣先曾论列，未赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1158391_comment'></div>况利州一路，累经灾伤，人民凋敝，全藉按察之官绥抚镇靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1158391_comment'></div>其熙辅所为如此，岂宜久居是职，必恐别生事端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1158391_comment'></div>欲望朝廷选差廉敏才识之士，充本路转运，以安远民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1158391_comment'></div>如杨佐显有赃私罪犯，即令本路提刑司体量虚实事状闻奏，依条施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1158391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。请替换利州路转运提刑张经。作品：再请选转运提刑。<div id='poem_1158392' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158392' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158392?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再请选转运提刑奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（皇祐四年二月知谏院时作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158392")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158392_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158392'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158392'>臣伏见诸路转运使并提点刑狱，自来朝廷凡有差除，皆以资序叙迁，或用臣僚荐举，閒容滥进，未甚得人，致一方之民必受其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158392_comment'></div>如李熙辅、张经等，居按察之任，当一路之重，不能遵守诏敕，振举职业，而挟私逞憾，无所畏惮，妄构刑狱，恣行追摄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158392_comment'></div>虽已冲替，未足惩戒，各乞重行黜降，以警将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158392_comment'></div>所有宣州廖询、秀州边瑀不公事迹，中外传闻，昨因安抚奏劾，方此彰露，而本路提、转殊失按举，居职不称，合正朝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158392_comment'></div>臣欲望圣慈应今后差转运使、提点刑狱臣僚，并请选素有才能公直廉明之人充职，不以资序深浅为限，则逐路得人，而官吏有所凛畏矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1158392_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　任兵部员外郎、知谏院。因刘兼济“才庸识暗，素无廉节”而上疏请求将其罢免。作品：请罢知雄州刘兼济。<div id='poem_1158460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢知雄州刘兼济奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158460")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158460'>臣近以新差知雄州刘兼济材庸识闇，素无廉节，当此边寄，中外之议，共以为不可，乞选有材略武臣充替，至今未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158460_comment'></div>臣伏见圣虑，以河朔事体至重，故进任大臣，节制一路，诚为长策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158460_comment'></div>然沿边守将未甚得人，此不可不精择也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158460_comment'></div>如祖宗朝用何继筠、李汉超、何承矩、李允则以御北鄙，皆极一时之选，是致边方宁肃，朝廷无北顾之忧，盖委任得人之明效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158460_comment'></div>方今不患乏材，但患不能用尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158460_comment'></div>缘雄州最为控扼重地，尤不当轻授，事机少失，虽悔何及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158460_comment'></div>且戎虏之性，诡诈万状，殊不可测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1158460_comment'></div>今既无名构是衅隙，故必有为之谋者，可不熟虑而预防之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1158460_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特令检会臣前来劄子，早赐施行，庶免缓急误事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1158460_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7ed51a693b1044f8831c7b2396c049a4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7ed51a693b1044f8831c7b2396c049a4");'><span id='7ed51a693b1044f8831c7b2396c049a4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1062')">1056-1062年</a>，58-64岁</div><div id='7ed51a693b1044f8831c7b2396c049a4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年12月5日</a>　进右司郎中、权知开封府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年6月</a>　迁右谏议大夫、权御史中丞、兼理检使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　进右司郎中、权知开封府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　宋仁宗既连失褒、豫、鄂三王，更无皇子。自至和三年正月得疾，逾时不能御殿，中外忧恐。作品：请建太子。<div id='poem_1158360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1158360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1158360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请建太子奏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(23145, "北宋", "包拯", "poem_title_1158360")'>包拯</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1158360_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1158360_0'>① 嘉祐三年六月为右谏议大夫权御史中丞时作</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1158360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1158360'>臣伏读前史，见圣王之御天下也，初纂大业，即建储贰，盖所以安亿兆危疑之心，绝中外觊觎之望，乃有国之常典，而历代所遵守者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1158360_comment'></div>伏自陛下绍隆丕构，已逾三纪，仁孝恭俭之德，格于上下，孜孜求治，未尝一日少怠，兹固群臣仰望清光之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1158360_comment'></div>但以东宫虚位日久，天下之心忧危至切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1158360_comment'></div>虽前后臣僚论列者多矣，卒不闻有所处置，未审圣意持久不决者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1158360_comment'></div>夫万物皆有根本，而太子天下之根本也，根本不立，祸孰大焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1158360_comment'></div>今既皇嗣未降，亦当采诗人盘维之义，固天下根本之地，不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1158360_comment'></div>臣愿陛下特出宸断，密与执政大臣协议，精择宗室中亲而有德望，众所推重者，优以封爵，置在左右，日加训勖，仍与增补僚属，选用厚重方正之士，令就禁邸，谕以善道，益其闻见。<div class='inline'
